# Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
## Ministerial Resolution No. (125) of 2025 Concerning the Formation of a Committee for the Accreditation of Real Estate Appraisal Curricula and Training Bodies for Certified Real Estate Appraiser I (B) and Advanced Real Estate Appraiser (A)

The Minister of Commerce and Industry,
Having reviewed:
- Decree-Law No. (15) of 1979 regarding the Civil Service, and its amending laws,
- Decree-Law No. (68) of 1980 promulgating the Commercial Law, and its amending laws,
- Decree-Law No. (116) of 1992 regarding Administrative Organization and the Determination and Delegation of Competencies,
- Law No. (111) of 2013 regarding the Regulation of Commercial Shop Licenses,
- Law No. (1) of 2016 promulgating the Companies Law, and its amending laws,
- Law No. (39) of 2014 regarding Consumer Protection,
- Law No. (18) of 2018 regarding the Commercial Register,
- The Decree issued on April 4, 1979, regarding the Civil Service System, and its amending decrees,
- Decree No. (191) of 2015 regarding the Organization of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>,
- Decree No. 73 of 2024 on the Formation of the Cabinet, and its amending decrees,
- Council of Ministers Resolution No. (37/Ninth) of 2004 approving the procedures for regulating the real estate market and establishing a real estate clearing company,
- Ministerial Resolution No. 27 of 2015 promulgating the Executive Regulations of Law No. 39 of 2014 regarding Consumer Protection, and its amending resolutions.

- And upon Ministerial Resolution No. 287 of 2016 issuing the Executive Regulations of Law No. 1 of 2016 issuing the Companies Law, and its amending resolutions,
- And upon Ministerial Resolution No. (152) of 2023 concerning the regulation of the real estate appraiser profession and valuation service providers,
- And upon the proposal of the Undersecretary of the Ministry,
- And based on the requirements of the public interest.
- And pursuant to the powers vested in us.

**It is decided**

### Article One
A committee is formed under the chairmanship of the Undersecretary of the Ministry (female) and the membership of the following gentlemen:
1- Mr. Sulaiman Hamad Al-Bader <orig>سليمان حمد البدر</orig> as Vice-Chairman
2- Mr. Imad Ali Al-Faraj <orig>عماد علي الفرج</orig> as a member
3- Mr. Ahmed Abdul Latif Al-Luhaib <orig>أحمد عبد اللطيف اللهيب</orig> as a member
4- Mr. Abdullah Al-Awadhi <orig>عبد الله العوضي</orig> as a member

# Ministry of Information <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>
## Administrative Decision No. (21) of 2025 regarding the cancellation of the license for the electronic media outlet named (Al-Midan News <orig>الميدان نيوز</orig>)

The Assistant Undersecretary for the Press, Publishing, and Publications Sector:
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (8) of 2016 regulating electronic media,
- And Ministerial Resolution No. (100) of 2016 issuing the Executive Regulations of Law No. 8 of 2016 regulating electronic media,
- And Administrative Decision No. 655 of 2022 regarding the delegation of certain powers,
- And the electronic media license No. 2018/218 issued on 16/1/2018.
- And the request submitted by the license holder on 4/6/2025,
- And the letter from the Director of the Electronic Publishing Department <orig>مدير إدارة النشر الإلكتروني</orig> No. 35 dated 4/6/2025.
- And based on the requirements of the public interest.

**It is decided**

### Article One
The license No. 2018/218 for the media outlet "Al-Midan News <orig>الميدان نيوز</orig>" is hereby canceled by law, based on the request of the license holder, in implementation of the last paragraph of clause (8) of Article (16) of the aforementioned Law No. (8) of 2016 regulating electronic media.

### Article Two
The concerned parties shall be notified of this decision, and it shall be published on the Ministry's website and in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Assistant Undersecretary
for the Press, Publishing, and Publications Sector

Issued on: 16 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H
Corresponding to: 12 June 2025 AD

  "page_title": "Ministerial Resolutions from the Ministry of Social Affairs and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry",
  "document_date": "2025-06-15",
  "issue_number": 1743,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": [
    "ar"
  ],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Minister of Social Affairs and Women's and Children's Affairs <orig>وزير الشؤون الاجتماعية وشؤون المرأة والطفولة</orig>, Minister of Commerce and Industry, Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajil <orig>وزير التجارة والصناعة خليفة عبدالله العجيل</orig>",
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains two ministerial resolutions: one from the Ministry of Social Affairs amending the articles of the Kuwait Teachers Society, and another from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry establishing a committee for real estate appraisal curricula."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1743 Seventy-First Year 3
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H – 15/6/2025 G
</header>


- And upon Decree No. (50) of 2017 concerning the Ministry of Social Affairs.
- And upon Ministerial Resolution No. (1/13) of 1962 regarding the promulgation of the Kuwait Teachers Society.
- And upon Ministerial Resolution No. (61) of 2005 concerning the Model Articles of Association for Public Benefit Associations.
- And upon the minutes of the extraordinary General Assembly meeting of the Kuwait Teachers Society held on 21/4/2025 to amend the Society's Articles of Association in accordance with the model.
- And upon the memorandum of the Assistant Undersecretary for Social Development dated 28/5/2025.
- And after the presentation by the Undersecretary of the Ministry.
- And based on the requirements of the public interest.

**((It is decided))**

### Article (1)
The Articles of Association of the Kuwait Teachers Society shall be amended in accordance with the Model Articles of Association.

### Article (2)
The addition of the following objectives is approved:
- Contributing to raising the professional, social, cultural, and scientific level of the members and the Society in cooperation with experts and analysts, in a manner that benefits the teaching community and achieves the highest levels of awareness and self-development for this important segment of Kuwaiti society.
- Providing available educational, instructional, and recreational services to members.
- Holding seminars, conferences, forums, lectures, and courses that serve various cultural and educational topics and publishing them in a cultural magazine issued by the Society.

5- Ms. Al-Bandari Khalid Al-Anzi <orig>البندري خالد العنزي</orig>, Member and Rapporteur

### Article Two
The committee shall undertake the following competencies:
1- Determining the main points of the curricula related to real estate appraisal for the categories of Certified Real Estate Appraiser I (B) and Advanced Real Estate Appraiser (A) in accordance with Ministerial Resolution No. 152 of 2023.
2- Reviewing and approving the curriculum submitted by the training entity.

### Article Three
The committee shall convene upon the invitation of the Chairman or his deputy. The committee's meeting shall not be valid unless a majority of the members are present, including the Chairman or his deputy. The committee's decisions shall be issued by a majority vote of the members present. In the event of a tie, the side on which the Chairman voted shall prevail.

### Article Four
The term of the committee shall be six months from the date of issuance of this resolution, and it may be extended for a similar period upon its request.

### Article Five
In order to achieve the competencies entrusted to it, the committee may coordinate directly with and address the bodies subordinate to the Minister to provide the committee members with the data and information required for the committee's tasks. These bodies must provide what the committee members request. The members may also visit any of these bodies and review any documents or records related to their work tasks.

### Article Six
A financial remuneration shall be granted to the committee members in light of the terms and conditions decided by the Civil Service Council in its meeting No. (1) of 2024, held on 28/2/2024, regarding the disbursement of special remunerations for committees formed to carry out extraordinary work.

### Article Seven
All responsible officials, each within their own jurisdiction, shall implement this resolution. It shall come into force from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Minister of Commerce and Industry
Khalifa Abdullah Al-Ajil <orig>خليفة عبدالله العجيل</orig>

Issued on: 8 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H
Corresponding to: 4 June 2025 G

- Cultural, scientific, and educational cooperation with various bodies and institutions inside and outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, including cooperation with various bodies to visit different Arab and foreign countries to learn about the latest educational systems after obtaining the approval of the concerned authorities.
- Cooperation with the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> and the Ministry of Higher Education <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig> regarding the provision of educational and academic consultations for the development of the educational process and the defense of teachers' issues.
- Encouraging scientific and social research to increase competencies and facilitate the exchange of educational, social, and cultural information between the association and international Arab unions.
- Working to consolidate relations and strengthen scientific and cultural cooperation between teachers in Arab and friendly countries, especially between the members of the association and teachers residing in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>.

### Article (3)
The provisions of this decision shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the competent authorities shall be informed and shall implement its contents.

Minister of Social Affairs
and Family and Childhood Affairs
Dr. Amthal Hadi Al-Huwailah <orig>د. أمثال هادي الحويلة</orig>

Issued on: 6 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H
Corresponding to: June 2, 2025 AD

# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
## Resolution No. (102) of 2025
### Concerning the Renewal of the Securities Activities License for the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, and its executive regulations and their amendments;
- And the securities activities license certificate for the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig> No. (AP/2016/0016) issued on 04/07/2022;
- And upon the request of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig> to renew its securities activities license with the Authority;
- And based on the decision of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig> in its meeting No. (16) of 2025, held on 03/06/2025.

It is decided as follows:
### Article One
The securities activity license of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig> with the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> is renewed to practice the activity of a Clearing Agency <orig>وكالة مقاصة</orig> to provide:
- Securities depository service.
- Settlement and clearing service.

This is for a period of three years, renewable upon payment of the prescribed fees, effective from 04/07/2025.

### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this resolution, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Chairman of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>رئيس مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
Imad Ahmad Tifoni <orig>عماد أحمد تيفوني</orig>

Issued on: June 04, 2025 AD

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Decision No. (103) of 2025 regarding a special license to market a collective investment scheme established outside the State of Kuwait, granted to Kuwait Financial Centre Company (Markaz) for marketing shares of MKZ Development 53",
  "document_date": "2025-06-15",
  "issue_number": 1743,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": [
    "ar",
    "en"
  ],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Anwar Jassem Al-Mudhaf <orig>أنوار جاسم المضف</orig>",
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains Decision No. 103 of 2025, which grants Kuwait Financial Centre (Markaz) a license to market 35,000 shares of MKZ Development 53, a company established in the Cayman Islands, to professional clients within Kuwait."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1743, Seventy-First Year
5
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H – 15/6/2025 G
</header>



Has decided the following:

## Article One
Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig> is licensed to market 35,000 shares (only thirty-five thousand shares) of the company MKZ Development 53, through a private placement within the State of Kuwait. The company is established in the Cayman Islands, and the offer price shall be 1,000 Pound Sterling (only one thousand Pound Sterling) per share.

## Article Two
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait shall be offered to professional clients only, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Bylaws of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and Regulation of Securities Activities, and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription applications shall be:
- Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig>.

## Article Three
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.

## Article Four
The term of the marketing license is one year, renewable annually, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

## Article Five
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In the event of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, this decision shall be considered null and void.

## Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Head of the Supervision Sector
Anwar Jassem Al-Mudhaf <orig>أنوار جاسم المضف</orig>

Issued on: 11 June 2025 G

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1743 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H - 15/6/2025 G
6
</header>


- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-248), issued on 5/12/2024, which states that Plasmafy General Trading Company <orig>شركة بلازما فاي للتجارة العامة</orig> committed the following violation:
  - Practicing a commercial activity of management offices without a commercial license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

**It is decided**
**(Article One)**
To warn/ Plasmafy General Trading Company <orig>شركة بلازما فاي للتجارة العامة</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal area - Block (B) - Plot (B36), of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules applicable in this regard.

**(Article Two)**
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

**Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry**

**Issued on: 2 June 2025**

---

# Decision No. P.A.I. (31) of 2025
### Imposing an Administrative Penalty

**The Acting Director General**

**Having reviewed:**
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-242), issued on 4/12/2024, which states that The First United General Trading Company <orig>الشركة المتحدة الأولى للتجارة العامة</orig> committed the following violation:
  - Practicing a commercial activity of management and engineering offices without a commercial license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

**It is decided**
**(Article One)**
To warn/ The First United General Trading Company <orig>الشركة المتحدة الأولى للتجارة العامة</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal area - Block (B) - Plots (B25 - B26), of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules applicable in this regard.

**(Article Two)**
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

**Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry**

**Issued on: 2 June 2025**
<page_end>6</page_end>

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1743, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 AH – 15/6/2025 AD
7
</header>

- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General <orig>مدير عام</orig> of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure for violating industrial projects.
The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-242), issued on 4/12/2024, stating that Al-Nafisi Holding Company <orig>شركة النفيسي القابضة</orig> committed the following violation:
- Engaging in the commercial activity of management offices without a commercial license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations <orig>اللجنة الدائمة للمخالفات الصناعية</orig> in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General <orig>نائب المدير العام</orig> for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.

It is decided
(Article One)
To warn Al-Nafisi Holding Company <orig>شركة النفيسي القابضة</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal Area <orig>منطقة المستقبل</orig> – Plot (B) <orig>قطعة (B)</orig> – Parcel (B45-B46) <orig>قسيمة (B45-B46)</orig>, of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.
(Article Two)
This resolution shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>مدير عام الهيئة العامة للصناعة بالإنابة</orig>
Issued on: 2 June 2025 AD

# Resolution No. P.A.I. (32) of 2025 on Imposing an Administrative Penalty
## The Acting Director General <orig>المدير العام بالتكليف</orig>
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General <orig>مدير عام</orig> of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure for violating industrial projects.
The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-255), issued on 11/12/2024, stating that Al-Nadharati Hassan Company <orig>شركة النظاراتي حسن</orig> committed the following violation:
- Engaging in the commercial activity of management offices without a commercial license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations <orig>اللجنة الدائمة للمخالفات الصناعية</orig> in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General <orig>نائب المدير العام</orig> for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.

It is decided
(Article One)
To warn Al-Nadharati Hassan Company <orig>شركة النظاراتي حسن</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal Area <orig>منطقة المستقبل</orig> – Plot (B) <orig>قطعة (B)</orig> – Parcel (B30) <orig>قسيمة (B30)</orig>, of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.
(Article Two)
This resolution shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>مدير عام الهيئة العامة للصناعة بالإنابة</orig>
Issued on: 2 June 2025 AD

- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A3-168), issued on 27/11/2024, which states that Al-Reem Canteen <orig>كانتين الريم</orig> committed the following violations:
  - Engaging in an industrial/craft activity without a license.
  - Operating a canteen without a license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (495/2025/1) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.
### It is decided
(Article One)
To warn Al-Reem Canteen <orig>كانتين الريم</orig>.
Located at shop No. (1) in the Al-Rai <orig>الري</orig> area – Block (1) – Plot (1529), belonging to the heirs of the late Badr Hamad Al-Roumi <orig>بدر حمد الرومي</orig>, of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.
(Article Two)
This resolution shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry
Issued on: 2 June 2025 G

# PAI Resolution No. (34) of 2025
## On Imposing an Administrative Penalty
The Acting Director General
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation reports submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department Nos. (A1-241 / A1-240 / A1-239), issued on 4/12/2024, which state that the National Media Group for Publishing and Advertising Company <orig>شركة المجموعة الإعلامية الوطنية للنشر والإعلان</orig> committed the following violation:
  - There is no commercial license for the National Media Group Company.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (495/2025/1) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.
### It is decided
(Article One)
To warn the National Media Group for Publishing and Advertising Company <orig>شركة المجموعة الإعلامية الوطنية للنشر والإعلان</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal <orig>المستقبل</orig> area – Block (B) – Plot (B42-B43-B44), of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.
(Article Two)
This resolution shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry
Issued on: 2 June 2025 G

**(Article One)**
To warn Saqr Al-Sahra International General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة صقر الصحراء العالمية للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal area – Block (F) – Plot (F15), of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

**(Article Two)**
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

# Decision No. P.A.I. (37) of 2025
## Regarding the Imposition of an Administrative Penalty

The Acting Director General
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-229), issued on 4/12/2024, which states that Sour Al-Dabbous Real Estate Company <orig>شركة سور الدبوس العقاري</orig> committed the following violation:
- Absence of a commercial license at the address.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (495/2025/1) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services <orig>نائب المدير العام للمواصفات والخدمات الصناعية</orig>.
And in the public interest.

**It is decided**

**(Article One)**
To warn Sour Al-Dabbous Real Estate Company <orig>شركة سور الدبوس العقاري</orig>.
Located in the Al-Mustaqbal area – Block (B) – Plot (B3), of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (3 months). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

**(Article Two)**
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>مدير عام الهيئة العامة للصناعة بالإنابة</orig>

Issued on: 2 June 2025 G

# Resolution No. P.A.I. (43) of 2025
## Imposing an Administrative Penalty

The Acting Director General
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A2-263), issued on 15/12/2024, which states that Al-Fintas International Company for Wholesale and Retail Trade <orig>شركة الفنطاس العالمية لتجارة الجملة والتجزئة</orig> committed the following violation:
- Leasing the industrial establishment or craft to a third party.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.

It is decided
(Article One)
To warn / Al-Fintas International Company for Wholesale and Retail Trade <orig>شركة الفنطاس العالمية لتجارة الجملة والتجزئة</orig>.
Located in the South Amghara area – Plot (1) – Parcel (29) – of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of (one month). In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

(Article Two)
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1743 Seventy-first Year 13 Sunday 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 AH – 15/6/2025 AD
</header>


- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure for violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A2-259), issued on 2/12/2024, stating the commission by / BBL Global Middle East Company <orig>شركة بي بي ال جلوبال ميدل ايست</orig> of the following violation:
  - The plot is closed by the concerned party.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by Mr. / Deputy Director General for Specifications and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

Has decided

### (Article One)
To warn / BBL Global Middle East Company <orig>شركة بي بي ال جلوبال ميدل ايست</orig>.
Located in the Sulaibiya Industrial Expansion area <orig>توسعة حرفية الصليبية</orig> – Block (1) – Plot (B48) – of the necessity to rectify the violation mentioned above within a maximum period of (one month). In the event the violation is not rectified, stricter measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

### (Article Two)
This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>

Issued on: 2 June 2025 AD

  - The plot is closed by the concerned party.

Located in the Sulaibiya Industrial Expansion area <orig>توسعة حرفية الصليبية</orig> – Block (1) – Plot (B49) – of the necessity to rectify the violation mentioned above within a maximum period of (one month). - Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry to impose the penalties of warning and closure on violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A2-261), issued on 12/12/2024, which states that Al-Alamia for Buildings Co. W.L.L. <orig>الشركة العالمية للمباني ذ.م.م</orig> committed the following violation:
    - The factory is not operational.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

**It has been decided**

### (Article One)

To warn Al-Alamia for Buildings Co. W.L.L. <orig>الشركة العالمية للمباني ذ.م.م</orig>.
Located in the Amghara Industrial Area <orig>منطقة امغره الصناعية</orig> – Block (3) – Plot (254) – of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of one (1) month. In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

### (Article Two)

This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry

Issued on: 2 June 2025 G

# Decision No. P.A.I. (47) of 2025
## Regarding the Imposition of an Administrative Penalty

The Acting Director General

**Having reviewed:-**
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry to impose the penalties of warning and closure on violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A2-260), issued on 12/12/2024, which states that Umm Al-Maradim Aluminum Workshops Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة ام المرادم لورش الالمنيوم ذ.م.م</orig> committed the following violation:
    - The plot is closed.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

**It has been decided**

### (Article One)

To warn Umm Al-Maradim Aluminum Workshops Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة ام المرادم لورش الالمنيوم ذ.م.م</orig>.
Located in the Amghara Industrial Area <orig>منطقة امغره الصناعية</orig> – Block (3) – Plot (161) – of the necessity to rectify the aforementioned violation within a maximum period of one (1) month. In the event of failure to rectify the violation, more severe measures will be taken in accordance with the rules in force in this regard.

### (Article Two)

This decision shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry

**(Article Two)**

This resolution shall be effective from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette, and the concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

</header>

- Ministerial Decision No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to impose the penalties of warning and closure on violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Environmental Control Department No. (C-53), issued on 4/12/2024, stating that the National Factory for Used Batteries and Metal Types <orig>المصنع الوطني للبطاريات المستهلكة وأصناف المعادن</orig> committed the following violations:
  - Inadequate ventilation in production and storage areas.
  - Improper storage of chemical materials in a manner that may cause them to react or emit pollutants.
  - Improper storage of batteries, leading to leakage outside the plot boundaries.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services.
And in the public interest.
## It is decided
### (Article One)
To close Plot No. (B9) located in the Jahra Industrial Expansion Area – Block (1) – belonging to the National Factory for Used Batteries and Metal Types <orig>المصنع الوطني للبطاريات المستهلكة وأصناف المعادن</orig>, until the violations and their resulting effects are removed.
### (Article Two)
In the event the violation is not removed within (one month) from the date of closure, a more severe penalty shall be imposed.
### (Article Three)
This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall be effective from the date of its issuance. The concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry
Issued on: 2 June 2025 G

- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to impose the penalties of warning and closure on violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A1-254), issued on 11/12/2024, stating that M/s Kohinoor Radiator Company for Radiator and Exhaust Repair <orig>شركة / راديتر كوهينور لتصليح راديتر وعادم السيارات</orig> committed the following violations:
  - Engaging in an industrial/craft activity without a license.
  - Presence of workers' housing with an area of 45 m² without a license.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services <orig>نائب المدير العام للمواصفات والخدمات الصناعية</orig>.
And in the public interest.

## It is decided

### (Article One)

To close shop No. (14) located in the Third Shuwaikh Industrial Area <orig>الشويخ الصناعية الثالثة</orig> – Block (B) – Plot (23), belonging to M/s Kohinoor Radiator Company for Radiator and Exhaust Repair <orig>شركة راديتر كوهينور لتصليح راديتر وعادم السيارات</orig>, until the violations and their resulting effects are rectified.

### (Article Two)

In the event the violation is not rectified after the passing of one (1) month from the date of closure, a more severe penalty shall be imposed.

### (Article Three)

This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall be effective from the date of its issuance. The concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>مدير عام الهيئة العامة للصناعة بالإنابة</orig>

Issued on: 2 June 2025 AD

# Decision No. PAI (61) of 2025 Regarding the Closure of a Plot

## The Acting Director General

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 regarding the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to impose the penalties of warning and closure on violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A4-120), issued on 16/12/2024, stating that Afkari Ghair Factory for Ready-Made Garments Production <orig>مصنع افكاري غير لإنتاج الملابس الجاهزة</orig> committed the following violation:
  - The unit is closed.
- Decision No. PAI (154) of 2020 issued on 22/11/2020, warning the aforementioned to rectify the violation within a maximum period of one (1) month from the date of the decision's issuance.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (1/2025/495) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General for Standards and Industrial Services <orig>نائب المدير العام للمواصفات والخدمات الصناعية</orig>.
And in the public interest.

## It is decided

### (Article One)

To close shop No. (M21) located in the Fahaheel area (Crafts Complex) <orig>الفحيحيل (المجمع الحرفي)</orig> – Block (5), belonging to M/s Afkari Ghair Factory for Ready-Made Garments Production <orig>مصنع افكاري غير لإنتاج الملابس الجاهزة</orig>, until the violations and their resulting effects are rectified.

### (Article Two)

In the event the violation is not rectified after the passing of one (1) month from the date of closure, a more severe penalty shall be imposed.

### (Article Three)

This decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall be effective from the date of its issuance. The concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>مدير عام الهيئة العامة للصناعة بالإنابة</orig>

Issued on: 2 June 2025 AD

# Resolution No. P.A.I. (63) of 2025 Regarding the Closure of a Plot

The Assigned Director General <orig>المدير العام بالتكليف</orig>

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (56) of 1996 concerning the issuance of the Industry Law, its executive regulations, and their amendments.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (5/2025) issued on 9/3/2025, authorizing the Director General <orig>المدير العام</orig> of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> to sign the penalties of warning and closure against violating industrial projects.
- The violation report submitted by the Industrial Inspection Department No. (A3-142), issued on 14/10/2024, which states that M/s. Penta Graphics for Manufacturing Neon and Plastic Signboards and Embossed and Animated Advertisements <orig>بينتا جرافيكس لتصنيع لوحات إعلانات النيون والبلاستيك والإعلانات البارزة والمتحركة</orig> committed the following violation:
  - Engaging in the activity of clothes printing without a license, while the existing license No. (202037) is for manufacturing signboards.
- The recommendation of the Permanent Committee for Industrial Violations in its meeting No. (495/1/2025) held on 08/01/2025.
- And based on the presentation by the Deputy Director General <orig>نائب المدير العام</orig> for Standards and Industrial Services.
- And in the public interest.

## It is decided

### (Article One)
To close shop No. (5) located in plot No. <orig>القسيمة رقم</orig> (1869) in the Al-Rai <orig>الري</orig> area – block <orig>قطعة</orig> (1), belonging to M/s. Penta Graphics for Manufacturing Neon and Plastic Signboards and Embossed and Animated Advertisements <orig>بينتا جرافيكس لتصنيع لوحات إعلانات النيون والبلاستيك والإعلانات البارزة والمتحركة</orig>, until the violations and their resulting effects are removed.

### (Article Two)
In the event the violation is not removed after one (month) from the date of closure, a more severe penalty shall be imposed.

### (Article Three)
This resolution shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall be effective from the date of its issuance. The concerned authorities shall implement it, each within its jurisdiction.

The correct version is: (Request for the division of a partnership company).

## Announcement
The owners of Le Churro Station for Snacks Company have submitted a request to the Partnership Companies Department <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> for the procedure of:
Request for the division of a partnership company

<table_caption>Company Capital Before and After Division</table_caption>
<table>
| Legal Entity | One-Person Company |
|---|---|
| Capital Before Division | 200 | Capital After Division | 100 |
</table>

Anyone with an objection is requested to file it with the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners, in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until their objection is decided by a final judgment.

# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
## Corrigendum
A typographical error was made by the requesting authority in Resolution No. (101) of 2025, published in Issue 1742 on Sunday, 8/6/2025. The error appeared in the first article, which stated: Resolution No. (92) of 2015 concerning the development of post-trade system infrastructures shall enter into force as of (13/07/2025).
The correct version is: Resolution No. (92) of 2025 concerning the development of post-trade system infrastructures shall enter into force as of (13/07/2025).
Therefore, we are republishing the resolution after correcting the error.

## Resolution No. (101) of 2025
Concerning the entry into force of the second part of the third phase of the Capital Market System Development Program

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, and its executive regulations and their amendments;
- And Resolution No. (60) of 2016 regarding the amendment of the executive regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010 on the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and its amendments, by adding the activity of a qualified securities broker registered with the stock exchange, issued on 27/06/2016;
- And Resolution No. (92) of 2025 concerning the development of post-trade system infrastructures;
- And the resolution of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig> issued in its meeting No. (09) of 2025 held on 26/03/2025, regarding the approval of the documents of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>;
- And the resolution of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig> issued in its meeting No. (13) of 2025 held on 14/05/2025, regarding the approval of the documents of the Kuwaiti Central Depository Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للإيداع المركزي</orig>;
- And the resolution of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig> issued in its meeting No. (16) of 2025 held on 03/06/2025, regarding the entry into force of the second part of the third phase of the Capital Market System Development Program.

Has decided the following:
### Article One
Resolution No. (92) of 2025 concerning the development of post-trade system infrastructures shall enter into force as of (13/07/2025).

### Article Two
All provisions contained in the following documents shall enter into force as of (13/07/2025):
1. The approved Rules of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
2. The approved Recovery Plan of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
3. The approved Failure Management and Procedures document, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
4. The approved Rules of the Kuwaiti Central Depository Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للإيداع المركزي</orig>, issued by the Kuwaiti Central Depository Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للإيداع المركزي</orig>.
5. The approved Governance document, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig> and its subsidiaries.

### Article Three
The following documents shall be repealed as of (13/07/2025):
1. The Financial Guarantee document, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
2. The Central Lending and Borrowing Rules, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
3. The Financial Guarantee document (Unlisted Securities Market), issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.

### Article Four
The application of the current approved documents shall remain in effect for a transitional period of six months from (13/07/2025):
1. The Rules of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
2. The Policies and Procedures Manual for General Assemblies via Electronic Systems, issued by the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>.
The application of these documents is limited to the purpose of regularizing the status of depository members only, as specified in the transitional provisions of the Central Depository Rules document issued by the Kuwaiti Central Depository Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للإيداع المركزي</orig> and referred to in Article One. The provisions of these documents shall not apply for any purpose other than this and the purpose specified in Article Five below.

### Article Five
The provisions of the documents referred to for repeal in Article Two above shall remain in effect for transactions executed before (13/07/2025).

### Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this resolution, each within its jurisdiction. It shall come into effect as of (13/07/2025) and be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Chairman of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority
Emad Ahmed Tifouni <orig>عماد أحمد تيفوني</orig>

Issued on: 4 June 2025 AD

# The Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الإجتماعية</orig>
## Announcement
The Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الإجتماعية</orig> announces a change in the closing date for Tender No. (PIFSS 1/M/5/2025) for the provision of operating licenses and the delivery of maintenance and technical support services for two Palo Alto 3410 devices at The Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الإجتماعية</orig>, which was previously announced in Issue No. (1742) on 8/6/2025. The new closing date will be Wednesday, 18/6/2025, instead of 19/6/2025. It is emphasized that bids must be submitted at the Institution's headquarters, and the deadline for submission is 1:00 PM.

Acting Director General <orig>المدير العام بالتكليف</orig>

## Announcement
The owners of the company / Tawazun Al-Jasad for the Management of Health Institutes <orig>توازن الجسد لادارة المعاهد الصحية</orig> ## The company is under liquidation, have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to proceed with the dissolution and liquidation of the company. Legal Entity: Limited Liability Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to file it with the Court of First Instance within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The filing of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on the objection.

The filing of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on the objection.

Anyone with an objection is requested to file it with the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. # Announcement
The owners of / Al-Rifaq Al-Kuwaitia Company for Fashion, Apparel, Footwear, and Jewelry Design <orig>شركة الرفاق الكويتية لتصميم الأزياء والملبوسات والأحذية والمجوهرات</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry to proceed with the dissolution and liquidation of the company. Legal Entity: One-Person Company.
Any party with an objection is requested to file a claim with the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. Filing an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until their objection is settled by a final judgment.

</table>

Any party with an objection to this is requested to contact the Commercial Licenses Department within fifteen days from the date of this announcement's publication. No objection will be accepted unless it is based on an enforceable court judgment or writ.

**Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وكيل وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>**

# Al Safat Investment Company <orig>شركة الصفاة للاستثمار</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned) Held on Monday, 2/6/2025

The adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of Al Safat Investment Company <orig>شركة الصفاة للاستثمار</orig> held its meeting at 1:00 PM on Monday, June 2, 2025, at the company's headquarters located in Hawalli <orig>حولي</orig> – Beirut Street – opposite Al-Qadsiah Club – Al Safat Building – 16th Floor.
The meeting was chaired by Mr. Ziad Tariq Al-Mukhazeem <orig>زياد طارق المخيزيم</orig> – Deputy Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer. The meeting was also attended by:–
- Shareholders holding 190,698,393 shares, in person and by proxy, representing 55.245% of the company's total share capital.
- The representative of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, Mr. Mohammed Salem Bu-Hadi <orig>محمد سالم بوهادي</orig>

**First:** The reduction of the authorized, issued, and paid-up capital from K.D. 38,327,568.800 to K.D. 31,752,228.800 was discussed. This is to be achieved by canceling 65,753,400 million shares at a nominal value of

Text after amendment:
The authorized, issued, and paid-up capital of the company is set at 31,752,228.800 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (thirty-one million, seven hundred fifty-two thousand, two hundred twenty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars and 800 fils), distributed over 317,522,288 shares (three hundred seventeen million, five hundred twenty-two thousand, two hundred eighty-eight shares) with a nominal value of 100 fils per share. All shares are in cash and in-kind, divided into a cash capital of 23,467,792.800 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (twenty-three million, four hundred sixty-seven thousand, seven hundred ninety-two Kuwaiti Dinars and 800 fils only) and an in-kind capital of 8,284,436 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (eight million, two hundred eighty-four thousand, four hundred thirty-six Kuwaiti Dinars only). This was approved by a vote of (100%).

Second: Approval was granted to amend Article (47) of the Articles of Association concerning the distribution of profits to shareholders, to read as follows:

Text before amendment:
A percentage of not less than ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal from the Board of Directors, to form a statutory reserve for the company. The Assembly may suspend this deduction if the statutory reserve exceeds half of the company's issued capital. Any amount deducted from the statutory reserve must be returned to it when the profits of subsequent years permit, unless this reserve exceeds half of the issued capital.
A percentage of the profits shall be deducted to meet the company's obligations under labor and social security laws.
A percentage not exceeding ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal from the Board of Directors, to form a voluntary reserve allocated for purposes determined by the Assembly.
The company may, based on a proposal from the Board of Directors and the approval of the Ordinary General Assembly, distribute profits to shareholders at the end of the fiscal year or on an interim basis (quarterly or semi-annually), provided that such distribution is from real profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and does not affect the company's paid-up capital.

Text after amendment:
A percentage of not less than ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal from the Board of Directors, to form a statutory reserve for the company. The Assembly may suspend this deduction if the statutory reserve exceeds half of the company's issued capital. Any amount deducted from the statutory reserve must be returned to it when the profits of subsequent years permit, unless this reserve exceeds half of the issued capital.
A percentage of the profits shall be deducted to meet the company's obligations under labor and social security laws.
A percentage not exceeding ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal from the Board of Directors, to form a voluntary reserve allocated for purposes determined by the Assembly.
The company may, based on a proposal from the Board of Directors and the approval of the Ordinary General Assembly, distribute profits to shareholders at the end of the fiscal year or on an interim basis (quarterly or semi-annually), provided that such distribution is from real profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and does not affect the company's paid-up capital. The General Assembly may, by a resolution determined annually, delegate authority to the Board of Directors and permit it to distribute these profits according to the aforementioned mechanism.
This was approved by a vote of (100%).
At the conclusion of the meeting, Mr. Ziad Tariq Al-Mukhayzim <orig>زياد طارق المخيزيم</orig> thanked all attendees, and the meeting ended at 1:30 PM.

Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer

# ACICO Industrial Company for Prefabricated Buildings and Constructions <orig>شركة أسيكو الصناعية للمباني الجاهزة والإنشاءات</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned)
## For the Fiscal Year Ending 31/12/2024

On Thursday, 29/5/2025 G, at 11:00 AM, at the factory headquarters of a subsidiary company (ACICO Industrial Company for Prefabricated Buildings and Constructions <orig>شركة أسيكو الصناعية للمباني الجاهزة والإنشاءات</orig>), located in the Sulaibiya Industrial Area <orig>منطقة الصليبية الصناعية</orig>, Plot 1, Block 8A, 8B, the adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly meeting of the shareholders of ACICO Industries Company (K.S.C.) Public was held. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Emad Abdullah Al-Essa <orig>عماد عبد الله العيسى</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors, and was attended by:
- Mr. Khalid Abdullah Al-Omari <orig>خالد عبدالله العمري</orig>, representing the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>
- Shareholders holding 183,507,157 shares in person and by proxy, representing 55.530% of the company's total shares of 333,400,095 shares.

After announcing that the legal quorum for the validity of the adjourned Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, the Chairman opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees and then proceeded to present the items on the agenda as follows:-

First: Approval was granted to amend Article (11) of the Company's Articles of Association
- Text before amendment:
"Each share entitles its owner to a share equal to that of others without distinction in the ownership of the company's assets and in the distributed profits as set out hereinafter."
- Text after amendment:
"Each share entitles its owner to a share equal to that of others without distinction in the ownership of the company's assets and in the distributed profits. However, the company may issue preferred shares, whereby some or all privileges may be granted to certain types of issued shares and to shares from an increase, in terms of voting, profits, liquidation proceeds, priority in payment of profits and capital, redemption of preferred shares, conversion rights, participation in surplus assets resulting from liquidation, or all of the foregoing combined, or otherwise, provided that shares of the same class are equal in rights, privileges, or restrictions. The rights, privileges, or restrictions related to a class of shares may not be amended except by a resolution of the Extraordinary General Assembly and with the approval of two-thirds of the holders of the class of shares to which the amendment relates."

In accordance with the following voting percentages:
<table_caption>Voting Results for Amending Article 11</table_caption>
<table>
| Agree | Disagree | Abstain |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 90.7% | 3.9% | 5.4% |
</table>

Second: Approval was granted to add a new article to the Articles of Association, numbered Article 54.
"The company's contract may provide for granting certain privileges or restrictions to certain types of shares, in terms of voting, profits, liquidation proceeds, or otherwise, provided that shares of that class are equal in rights, duties, privileges, or restrictions. The rights, privileges, or restrictions related to a class of shares may not be amended except by a resolution of the Extraordinary General Assembly and with the approval of two-thirds of the holders of the class of shares to which the amendment relates, in accordance with the conditions and rules for issuing preferred shares and their conversion into ordinary shares issued by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>, and the conditions and procedures for their redemption by the company. Preferred shares shall be traded in accordance with the conditions and rules for trading preferred shares issued by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>."

In accordance with the following voting percentages:

## Al-Nafisi National Real Estate Group Company K.S.C. (Closed)
### Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting for the Year Ended 31/12/2024
The Extraordinary General Assembly of Al-Nafisi National Real Estate Group Company K.S.C. (Closed) held its meeting at 2:30 PM on Sunday, 25/05/2025, at the company's headquarters – Al-Salhia Complex. After Mr. Nasser Saud Al-Munaie <orig>ناصر سعود المنيع</orig>, the representative of the Gulf Clearing Company, announced a legal quorum of 100% based on proxies and attendance, and in the presence of Mr. Nayef Al-Bazea <orig>نايف البزيع</orig> from the office of RSM Al-Bazea & Co., the company's auditor:
Approval was granted to amend Article No. (14) of the Articles of Association and its corresponding article in the Memorandum of Association, with a reservation from the Public Authority for Minors Affairs <orig>الهيئة العامة لشؤون القصر</orig>, represented by Mr. Hamad Al-Ainati <orig>حمد العيناتي</orig>, agent for Yahin Fawzi Al-Nafisi <orig>ياحين فوزي النفيسي</orig>, representing 3.9216% of the attendees, as follows:

### Article No. (14) Before Amendment:
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of (6 members) six members, elected by the General Assembly by secret ballot. The term of membership shall be three years, renewable. Any shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors in proportion to the shares they own. The number of board members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of board members to be elected. Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board of Directors, except to the extent that exceeds the percentage used to appoint their representatives on the Board. A group of shareholders may form an alliance among themselves to appoint one or more representatives on their behalf to the Board of Directors, in proportion to their combined ownership.
These representatives shall have the same rights and obligations as elected members, and the shareholder shall be responsible for the actions of their representatives towards the company, its creditors, and its shareholders.
If it is not possible to elect a new Board of Directors on the specified date, the existing Board shall continue to manage the company's business until the reasons preventing the election are resolved and a new Board of Directors is elected.

### Article No. (14) After Amendment:
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of (7 members) seven members, elected by the General Assembly by secret ballot. The term of membership shall be three years, renewable. Any shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors in proportion to the shares they own. The number of board members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of board members to be elected. Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board of Directors, except to the extent that exceeds the percentage used to appoint their representatives on the Board. A group of shareholders may form an alliance among themselves to appoint one or more representatives on their behalf to the Board of Directors, in proportion to their combined ownership.
These representatives shall have the same rights and obligations as elected members, and the shareholder shall be responsible for the actions of their representatives towards the company, its creditors, and its shareholders.
If it is not possible to elect a new Board of Directors on the specified date, the existing Board shall continue to manage the company's business until the reasons preventing the election are resolved and a new Board of Directors is elected.
The meeting concluded at 2:40 PM on Sunday, 25/05/2025.
Chairman of the General Assembly

## Real Estate Trade Centers Company (K.S.C.P.)
### Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
The Extraordinary General Assembly of the Real Estate Trade Centers Company (K.S.C.P.) was held on Sunday, 01/06/2025, at the company's headquarters located in the Qibla area – Mohammed Thunayan Al-Ghanem Street – Al-Salhia Commercial Complex – Entrance 2 – 1st Floor, at 11:00 AM, in the presence of shareholders representing 80.543% of the total number of shareholders, and in the presence of:
1- Engineer/ Talal Abdulhameed Dashti <orig>طلال عبدالحميد دشتي</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors (Chairman of the Assembly)
2- Mr. Khaled Abdullah Al-Omari <orig>خالد عبدالله العمري</orig> (Kuwait Clearing Company)
3- Mr. Mohamed Yahya Mohamed Abdo <orig>محمد يحيى محمد عبده</orig> (representing Mr. Ali Abdulrahman Al-Hasawi <orig>علي عبدالرحمن الحساوي</orig> from the auditing office Rödl Middle East Burgan, Chartered Accountants)
As the legal quorum for convening the Extraordinary General Assembly was met, Engineer/ Talal Abdulhameed Dashti <orig>طلال عبدالحميد دشتي</orig> chaired the session as Chairman of the Assembly to discuss the items on the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly, as follows:
Amending the text of Article (5) of the Memorandum of Association and Article (4) of the Articles of Association related to the company's objectives, in accordance with Ministerial Resolution No. (167) of 2022 regarding the regularization of the status of companies and commercial establishments according to the United Nations classification of commercial activities.

### Text Before Amendment:
The purposes for which the company was established are as follows:
01- Owning, selling, and purchasing real estate and land and developing them for the company's account inside and outside Kuwait, as well as managing third-party properties, leasing, and marketing real estate, all in a manner that does not violate the provisions stipulated in existing laws and the prohibition on trading in private housing plots as stipulated by these laws.
02- Owning, selling, and purchasing shares and bonds of real estate companies for the company's account only, in Kuwait and abroad.
03- Preparing studies and providing consultations in all types of real estate fields, provided that the required conditions are met by those who practice this service.
04- Owning and managing hotels, health and sports clubs, private hospitals, and tourist facilities, and leasing and renting them.
05- Carrying out maintenance work and all services related to buildings and properties owned by the company and by others, including maintenance work, and the execution of civil, mechanical, and electrical works, elevators, and air conditioning works, in a manner that ensures the preservation and safety of the buildings.
06- Managing, operating, investing in, and leasing hotels, clubs, motels, guesthouses, rest houses, parks, gardens, exhibitions, restaurants, cafeterias, residential complexes, tourist resorts, health hospitals, recreational and sports projects, and shops of various grades and levels, including all primary and ancillary services, attached facilities, and other necessary services.
07- Organizing real estate exhibitions for the company's real estate projects, in accordance with the regulations in force at the Ministry.
08- Owning and managing commercial markets and residential complexes.
09- Conducting real estate auctions according to the applicable regulations.
10- Utilizing the company's available financial surpluses by investing them in financial and real estate portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities.
11- Direct contribution to establishing the infrastructure for residential, commercial, industrial, tourist, urban, and sports areas and projects under the Build-Operate-Transfer (BOT) system, and managing real estate facilities under the (BOT) system, whether for the company's benefit or for others.
12- Providing real estate project management services and preparing related studies.

# International Financial Investments Holding Company (K.S.C.P.) <orig>شركة الاستثمارات المالية الدولية القابضة (ش. م. ك. ع)</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
### For the Fiscal Year Ended 31/12/2024

On Sunday, May 25, 2025, at 11:30 AM, the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting of the International Financial Investments Holding Company (K.S.C.P.) <orig>شركة الاستثمارات المالية الدولية القابضة (ش.م.ك.ع)</orig> was held at the company's headquarters located in the Kuwait Market <orig>سوق الكويت</orig> building – 8th Floor – Meeting Hall, via the General Assembly meeting system of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>, with the attendance of:

2) Mr. Khaled Saleh Ghoneim <orig>خالد صالح غنيم</orig> – from the office of Al-Qatami & Al-Aiban & Partners Grant Thornton <orig>مكتب القطامي والعيبان وشركاهم جرانت ثورنتون</orig> (Auditor)

(K.S.C.)
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
## For the fiscal year ending 31/12/2024

On Thursday, May 22, 2025, at 11:16 AM, the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting of the International Kuwaiti Investment Holding Company <orig>الشركة الدولية الكويتية للاستثمار القابضة</orig> (K.S.C.) was held at the company's headquarters located in Sharq — Ahmed Al-Jaber Street — Arzan Tower — Fourth Floor, via the electronic platform of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig> through electronic means, in the presence of:
1) Mr. Hamed Mohammed Al-Eiban <orig>حامد محمد العيبان</orig> - Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer (Chairman of the Meeting)
2) Mr. Khaled Saleh Ghaith <orig>خالد صالح غيث</orig> — from the office of Al-Qatami & Al-Aiban and Partners Grant Thornton (Auditor)

Shareholders representing 38,706,352 shares out of the total capital of 50,291,951 shares attended, with an attendance rate of 77.470%, after excluding 328,925 treasury shares.

After the Chairman of the Meeting announced that the legal quorum for holding the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, the Assembly began discussing the agenda items, which resulted in the following resolutions:

1. Approval by a majority of 55.441% of the company's issued and paid-up capital of the Board of Directors' proposal to increase the authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital from KWD 5,029,195.325 (five million, twenty-nine thousand, one hundred ninety-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and 325 fils), representing 50,291,953 shares, to KWD 6,286,494.100 (six million, two hundred eighty-six thousand, four hundred ninety-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and 100 fils), representing 62,864,941 shares. This is to be done by distributing bonus shares at a rate of 25% of the company's authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital, amounting to 12,572,988 shares, to be distributed to the shareholders registered in the company's records as of the date of the Ordinary General Assembly meeting for the fiscal year ending 31/12/2024. The Assembly authorizes the Board of Directors to determine the methods and timing of the increase, handle fractional shares, and all procedures related to this increase.
2. Approval by a majority of 55.441% of the company's issued and paid-up capital of the Board of Directors' proposal to amend Article (6) of the Memorandum of Association and Article (5) of the Articles of Association of the company as follows:

**Text before amendment:**
"The authorized, issued, and paid-up capital of the company is set at KWD 5,029,195.325 (five million, twenty-nine thousand, one hundred ninety-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and 325 fils), divided into 50,291,953 shares, with a nominal value of 100 (one hundred) fils per share, fully paid, and all shares are in cash."

**Text after amendment:**
"The authorized, issued, and paid-up capital of the company is set at KWD 6,286,494.100 (six million, two hundred eighty-six thousand, four hundred ninety-four Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and 100 fils), divided into 62,864,941 shares, with a nominal value of 100 (one hundred) fils per share, fully paid, and all shares are in cash."

After concluding the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly, the Chairman of the Meeting announced the end of the assembly at 11:30 AM, after thanking everyone for their cooperation.

Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer

# Kuwaiti Indian Holding Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الكويتية الهندية القابضة ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting

The Extraordinary General Assembly of the Kuwaiti Indian Holding Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية الهندية القابضة</orig> (K.S.C.C.) was held at 11:15 AM on Monday, 02/06/2025, in the Shuwaikh area – intersection of Jahra Street and Airport Road – Noor Financial Investment Building – next to the National Industries Group.

The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> was notified of the agenda, date, and location of the Ordinary General Assembly meeting by letter dated 11/05/2025.

In accordance with the provisions of the Companies Law No. (1) of 2016.

The meeting was chaired by Mr. Fahad Bader Abdulrahman Al-Bader <orig>فهد بدر عبدالرحمن البدر</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors.

Shareholders holding 16,230,343 shares by proxy also attended, representing 77.288% (after excluding 353 treasury shares) of the company's total shares of 21,000,000.

After announcing that the legal quorum required for the validity of the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, Mr. Fahad Bader Abdulrahman Al-Bader <orig>فهد بدر عبدالرحمن البدر</orig> – Chairman of the Meeting, opened the session, welcoming the attendees. The Extraordinary General Assembly proceeded to discuss the items on the agenda sequentially as listed:

**First: – Approval was granted to amend Article No. (5) of the Memorandum of Association and Article No. (4) of the Articles of Association to read as shown below:**

**Text before amendment:**
The purposes for which the company was established are as follows:-
1. Owning shares in Kuwaiti or foreign shareholding companies, as well as owning shares or stakes in Kuwaiti or foreign limited liability companies, or participating in the establishment, management, lending to, and guaranteeing of these companies of both types with third parties.
2. Investing its funds in trading stocks, bonds, and other securities.
3. Lending to companies in which it owns shares and guaranteeing them with third parties. In this case, the holding company's participation in the capital of the borrowing company must not be less than 20%.
4. Owning industrial property rights such as patents, industrial trademarks, industrial designs, or any other related rights, and leasing them to other companies for exploitation, whether inside or outside Kuwait.
5. Owning the movable assets necessary to conduct its activities within the limits permitted by law.
6. Utilizing the company's available financial surpluses by investing them in financial portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities.

The company may conduct the aforementioned business in the State of Kuwait and abroad, either directly or through an agent.

The company may have an interest in or associate in any way with entities that carry out activities similar to its own or that may assist it in achieving its objectives in Kuwait or abroad, and it may establish, participate in, purchase, or affiliate with such entities.

**Text after amendment:**
The purposes for which the company was established are as follows:-

Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H - 15/6/2025 G
44
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1743, Seventy-first Year
