Second: Approval was granted to amend the text of Article (47) – (Amended) of the company's Articles of Association to read as shown below:
Text before amendment:
1- A percentage of not less than ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal by the Board of Directors, to form a statutory reserve for the company. The Assembly may suspend this deduction if the statutory reserve exceeds half of the company's issued capital.
2. A percentage not exceeding ten percent of the net profits may be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal by the Board of Directors, to form an optional reserve allocated for purposes determined by the Assembly.
3. The Ordinary General Assembly must decide to deduct a percentage of the profits to meet the obligations incumbent upon the company under labor and social security laws. A special fund may be established to assist the company's workers and employees.
Text after amendment:
The net profits shall be distributed as follows:
1 – A percentage of not less than ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted annually, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly based on a proposal by the Board of Directors, to form a statutory reserve for the company. The Assembly may suspend this deduction if the statutory reserve exceeds half of the company's issued capital.
The statutory reserve may only be used to cover the company's losses or to secure the distribution of dividends to shareholders at a rate not exceeding five percent of the paid-up capital in years when the company's profits do not permit the distribution of this percentage, due to the absence of an optional reserve that would allow for the distribution of this percentage of profits. Whatever is deducted from the statutory reserve must be returned to it when the profits of subsequent years permit, unless this reserve exceeds half of the issued capital.
2 – A percentage of 1% (one percent) of the company's annual net profits shall be deducted for the benefit of the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig> in accordance with the Amiri Decree issued on December 12, 1976.
All amendments are subject to the approval of the competent regulatory authorities.
The chairman of the meeting extended his sincere thanks to the attending shareholders, and the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting concluded at 11:25 AM on the same day.
Chairman of the Board of Directors

...shall continue to manage the company's business until the reasons cease to exist and a new board is elected.
A candidate for membership of the Board of Directors must meet the following conditions:
1- To have the legal capacity to act.
2- Not to have been previously convicted of a felony with a penalty restricting freedom, or a crime of bankruptcy by negligence or fraud, or a crime against honor or trust, or a penalty restricting freedom for violating the provisions of this law, unless he has been rehabilitated.
3- With the exception of independent board members, he must personally own, or the person he represents must own, a number of the company's shares.
If a board member loses any of the preceding conditions or other conditions stipulated in this law or other laws, his membership status shall be revoked from the date of losing that condition.
Addition of Article No. (55)
The relevant regulatory authorities shall establish corporate governance rules for the companies under their supervision, in a manner that achieves the best protection and balance between the interests of the company's management, its shareholders, and other related stakeholders. They shall also specify the conditions to be met by independent members of the Board of Directors.
Addition of Article No. (56)
Regulatory authorities may require companies under their supervision to have among their board members one or more independent members with experience and competence, to be elected by the Ordinary General Assembly, which shall determine their remuneration in accordance with governance rules, provided that their number does not exceed half of the board members. It is not required for an independent member to be a shareholder in the company.
Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
## Announcement
The General Directorate of Nationality and Travel Documents <orig>الإدارة العامة للجنسية ووثائق السفر</orig> announces that the persons listed below claim to have lost their Kuwaiti passports. Anyone who finds any of them is requested to hand them over to the Directorate within two weeks from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette. Otherwise, these persons will be issued new Kuwaiti passports according to the established procedures.

# Universal Navigation Company <orig>شركة يونيفيرسال للملاحة</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
On Wednesday, 04/06/2025, at 10:00 AM, at the company's headquarters located in the Qibla area <orig>منطقة القبلة</orig>, Fahad Al-Salem Street <orig>شارع فهد السالم</orig>, Akhwan Tower <orig>برج اخوان</orig>, 23rd floor.
Mr. Khalifa Ahmed Al-Jassem <orig>خليفة احمد الجاسم</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer – opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees. The total shares of those present amounted to 30,000,000 shares, representing 100% of the company's total shares of 30,000,000.
It was agreed to amend Article (14) and add Article (55) and Article (56) to the Articles of Association as follows:
Text of the Article in the Articles of Association before amendment – Article No. (14)
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors composed of (6) six members elected by the General Assembly by secret ballot. If it is not possible to elect a new Board of Directors on the specified date, the existing Board shall continue

### Notice
Regarding the amendment of the closing date (submission of bids) for Practice No. (L.A 231 /2024 . 2025) for the comprehensive operation and maintenance of the traffic management system on the road network for the General Department of Traffic – at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
Please be advised that the closing date (submission of bids) for the aforementioned practice has been extended to Wednesday, 16/7/2025, at the Bid Opening Committee in the Ministry of Interior building (Sharq area – Al-Siddiq School – First Floor), from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM. No bids submitted before or after the specified time will be accepted.

### Announcement
The Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> announces Practice No. (L.Sh 2025/7-2026) for the supply of personal workstation computers, Minilab photo printing devices, and other accessories for the Criminal Photography Section at the Crime Scene Department – for the General Department of Criminal Evidence, for the General Department of Information Systems, at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
Companies/institutions specialized in this field should visit the General Department of Financial Affairs – Tenders Department (in Ardiya Industrial Area) to obtain the documents for this practice for a fee of 20 KWD (Twenty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) (via K-Net) (non-refundable). A preliminary guarantee (to be attached to the financial bid for the practice) must be submitted for each item separately as follows:
1. Preliminary insurance amount for the first item: 900 KWD
2. Preliminary insurance amount for the second item: 8 KWD
3. Preliminary insurance amount for the third item: 110 KWD
4. Preliminary insurance amount for the fourth item: 30 KWD
5. Preliminary insurance amount for the fifth item: 90 KWD
6. Preliminary insurance amount for the sixth item: 25 KWD
7. Preliminary insurance amount for the seventh item: 5 KWD
Note that the final insurance for the practice is 10% of the total contract value.
Applicants must bring a copy of the practice announcement from the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), and the following documents:
- A valid registration receipt from the Ministry of Interior.
Or
- A registration request to register with the Ministry and then purchase the practice documents.

# Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>
## Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>) announces the following tenders:
<table_caption>Tender Details for Medical Supplies (Announcement 1)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Tender No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date | Publication Date |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | 5PC003 | Special materials for pediatric and neonatal departments for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 300 | 7/7/2025 | 15/6/2025 |
| 2 | 4DB068 | Intravenous solution sets for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 1000 | 14/7/2025 | 15/6/2025 |
| 3 | 5DB001 | Connectors for purifying intravenous solutions for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 1000 | 14/7/2025 | 15/6/2025 |
| 4 | 5DAN23 | Consumables for the Anesthesia and Intensive Care Departments Council for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 150 | 14/7/2025 | 15/6/2025 |
| 5 | 5D1007 | Sterile, powder-free LATEX surgical gloves, size 6.5, for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 150 | 14/7/2025 | 15/6/2025 |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the tender must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry.
3- When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Botanical Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنياتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and the product's registration in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, included with the submitted bid (specific to drug control).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product being requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the relevant control authority (Medicines – Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's website.
8- The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, inclusive of the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's website.

# Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> announces Tender No. S/MS/12/2025/2026 for the supply of a student health file, open to companies and institutions specialized in this field, in accordance with the general and special conditions detailed in the tender documents, which can be obtained from the Ministry's website (www.moh.gov.kw) for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.), only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
It is required to attach a letter from the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> when submitting the booklet, confirming compliance with the National Labor Support Law, in accordance with Law No. 19 of 2000 and Council of Ministers Decision No. 1104/Fifth of 2008 regarding the support and encouragement of national labor.
The closing date is at 1:00 PM on Monday, 30/06/2025, at the tender box in the main office of the Ministry of Health (Sulaibikhat – Ministry of Health building – First Floor – Procurement Department – Tenders Section). Bids shall be valid for the duration of the tender validity period.
Bids must be valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date. The initial bid bond is (2%), only two percent, of the bid value, valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity.
Note: Priority will be given to small and medium-sized enterprises affiliated with the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development.

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Health

Companies wishing to participate in the tender must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered in the supplier registry with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>.
2- The local company must be specialized in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Herbal Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and the product's registration in the supplier registry at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to drug control).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product being requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the relevant control authority (Medicines – Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a national labor support percentage certificate.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.
8- The fees for purchasing the tender booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, inclusive of the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.

2- The local company must be specialized in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Botanical Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنياتية</orig> or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and substance's registration in the Suppliers Register <orig>سجل الموردين</orig> at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, included within the submitted bid (specific to Pharmaceuticals Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product being requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the relevant control unit (Pharmaceuticals - Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a national labor support percentage certificate.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, inclusive with the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

# Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee, held on 20/05/2025

The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/69 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 1650/2021, has convened.
- Mr. / Director of the Central Registry for Births and Deaths <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig>, Chairman
- Dr. / Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig>, Member
- Ms. / Head of the Research and Opinion Department <orig>قسم البحوث والرأي</orig>, Member
- Mr. / Head of the Registration Department <orig>قسم القيد</orig>, Member
- Mr. / Head of the Deaths Department <orig>قسم الوفيات</orig>, Member
- Mr. / The Legal Researcher <orig>الباحث القانوني</orig>, Member

The secretarial duties of the committee were performed by Ms. Shukriya Al-Durai'i <orig>شكرية الدريعي</orig>.

The Committee reviewed requests from No. ((199)) to No. ((204)) in the attached list, concerning the amendment of data in the birth and death records for requests of unregistered births and deaths. After examination and verification that all documents and papers are complete, the Committee decides to announce the amendments and requests in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) for two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement passes without any objection being submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers, and the birth and death certificates will be issued.

- Head of the Research and Opinion Department
- Head of the Registration Department
- Head of the Deaths Department
- Head of the General Medical Council
- Director of the Central Registry for Births
- Committee Secretary# Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>

# Announcement of Public Auction of Movable Property
The Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>, Farwaniya Court <orig>محكمة الفروانية</orig>, announces the sale by public auction of the movable property described below, in execution of the judgment issued in enforcement file No. (242165180)
in favor of / Commercial Bank of Kuwait <orig>البنك التجاري الكويتي</orig>
against / Malas Bu Khammas Restaurant Company (W.L.L.) <orig>شركة مطعم ملاس بو خماس (ذ.م.م)</orig>
The sale will take place at the defendant's premises located in Jleeb Al-Shuyoukh <orig>جليب الشيوخ</orig> – Block 4 – Street 250 – Plot 900026 – next to the slaughterhouse – PACI No. (93550385)
on Monday, 7/7/2025, at 10:00 AM, in execution of the judgment.
Description of Movable Property:-
1- Nineteen (19) floor-standing gas stoves.
2- Two (2) 6-burner stoves with legs + one (1) 4-burner stove.
3- Six (6) double-door display refrigerators.
4- Thirteen (13) double-door steel freezers + one (1) single-door freezer.
5- Thirty-five (35) large steel tables with legs.
6- Two (2) double-door steel food warmers + one (1) single-door food warmer with legs for keeping food warm after cooking.
7- Three (3) 3-door steel ovens, Wibur brand.
8- Twenty-four (24) cooking pots of various sizes.
9- Forty (40) steel food warmers of various shapes with lids for serving.
10- Twenty-five (25) steel serving dishes with lids of various sizes.
11- Thirty (30) food warmers without lids.
12- One (1) electric deep fryer.
13- Three (3) computers (monitor + hard disk) of various brands, black in color.

Head of the Farwaniya Governorate Enforcement Department

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1743, Seventy-First Year
57
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H – 15/6/2025 G
</header>

2- Shua'a Mubarak Saad Al-Qabba <orig>شعاع مبارك سعد القبا</orig>.

Versus:
1- Sa'da Mohammed Al-Mukhalaf <orig>سعده محمد المخلف</orig>.
2- Director of the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>مدير إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>, in his capacity.
3- Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وكيل وزارة العدل</orig>, in his capacity.
4- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.

## First: Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
- Property under Document No. 3851/1983, located in the Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> area – Block 3 – Plot No. 105 – from Plan No. T M /2/11/ 325– 3 B – with an area of 750 m2.
*Inspection:
On 17/10/2022, we proceeded to the Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> area, Block 3, Al-Qasr, Street 3, Avenue 6, Plot 105, House 2, from Plan No. (T M / 11 / 2/ 325 –3 B), automated number for the disputed property 14266117, to inspect the disputed property on-site in the presence and under the guidance of the two claimants in person, and with the assistance of the study expert, Mr. Saad Mubarak Al-Mutairi <orig>سعد مبارك المطيري</orig>, appointed by the Administration. The inspection was conducted as follows:
- The disputed property is a house clad in beige-colored stone, consisting of a ground floor and a first floor. It is located on a corner with two streets and has adjoining neighbors on the remaining sides. The property has two annexes on the facades of the house, one on the side street and one on the front street. There is a large setback for the property on the front street side, and there is an internal courtyard.
- The disputed property conforms, in terms of general and specific specifications, to Document No. 3851, registered on 24/4/1983, with an area of 750 m2, as stated in the contract (Proof of Ownership by Inheritance and Buyout in Exchange for Consideration) issued by the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>, Real Estate Registration and Documentation Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>.
- The ground floor consists of 5 rooms, 3 bathrooms, a kitchen, a large living hall, and another hall with a preparation counter.
- The annex located on the side street consists of 3 rooms, 2 bathrooms, and a kitchen, and is used as a diwaniya.
- The annex located on the front street consists of 2 rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen, and is rented out to a third party. The two claimants described its components to the expert.
- The first floor consists of two apartments rented out to third parties. The apartment on the side street consists of a living hall, two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen. The apartment on the front street consists of 3 rooms, 2 bathrooms, and a kitchen. The two claimants described the components of the two apartments to the expert.
- The air conditioning in the disputed property is central air on the ground floor, and split-unit and window-unit air conditioning on the first floor and in the annexes.
- The expert asked the two claimants about the occupant of the property in question and who has clear possession of it. They stated that their mother, the first defendant, resides in it with her daughter, and that her son and his family have been paying them rent in recent years. There are also tenants in the property, as previously stated.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at a base price of KWD 473,850 (four hundred seventy-three thousand, eight hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a payment of at least one-fifth of this price is required by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at his own risk during the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at his own risk on the basis of the price that was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. The parties initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to execute a lease contract in his favor for a similar rent."

Deputy President of the Court of First Instance

<page_start>58</page_start>
<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Expert Report on Share Valuation in Case No. 159/2023",
  "document_date": "2025-06-15",
  "issue_number": 1743,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": [
    "ar"
  ],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page details an expert's valuation of shares in Mahmoud Haider and Sons Co. for legal case No. 159/2023, outlining the methodology, findings, case parties, and key dates."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
58 Sunday 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H - 15/6/2025 AD
</header>
With reference to the assignment by the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> pursuant to the judgment issued in Case No. 159/2023 Sales / 3 dated November 23, 2023, regarding the appointment of an auditor (expert) certified by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> to prepare a report study determining the fair value of the shares owned by Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ م م</orig>, amounting to one share, as of December 31, 2023.
After reviewing the case file and the documents submitted by Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. (W.L.L.) <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات (ذ.م.م)</orig>, including an amendment to the articles of association of a limited liability company dated July 9, 2019, it is clear to us that the share of Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> consists of one share, representing 1% of the total shares of the company.
In light of the information and data obtained from the management and due to the limited purpose of the information received, the information may be incomplete. Therefore, the management of the company under valuation has undertaken to provide this data and information as correct without any verification.
Based on our analysis of the information presented in this report, the underlying assumptions, and using the net asset value method, the net asset value as of December 31, 2023, was concluded. Consequently, the fair market value of the equity in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023, is 7,294,211 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seven million, two hundred ninety-four thousand, two hundred and eleven Kuwaiti Dinars).
The fair market value of the share of Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023, is an amount of 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seventy-two thousand, nine hundred forty-two Dinars and eleven Kuwaiti fils) = 7,294,211 ÷ 100 = 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars, with attention drawn to the following:
a) There is a debit balance due from Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in the amount of 1,341,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, according to the data received from the company, listed under the related parties' debit balance as of December 31, 2023.
b) According to the documents reviewed, submitted by the management of Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig>, a document dated December 27, 2020, was reviewed. It is a contract for the dissolution of a limited liability company pursuant to an appellate court judgment. The legal opinion issued by the Minister of Justice on June 14, 2022, was adopted, under which the share of Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> was amended, making him the owner of 33 shares instead of one share. Accordingly, if this amendment is taken into account, the total value of these 33 shares would be 2,407,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (two million, four hundred seven thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinars and sixty-three fils). Consequently, the net amount outstanding to Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> becomes 1,066,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one million, sixty-six thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinars and sixty-three fils) after deducting the debit balance due from him as of December 31, 2023.
In accordance with the court's decision regarding the appointment of the expert dated November 23, 2023, which is to estimate the value of only one share, we have valued the company and determined the value of the single share of Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig>. The matter is left to the court to consider the documents and other issued judgments.
This study should be read in light of the required assignment concerning the preparation of a study to determine the fair value of the shares owned by Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023. This study has been prepared in good faith based on the technical and financial information provided by the management of Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of the date of this study, without any independent verification and/or due diligence of said data/information. The study is confidential, and no one has the right to quote it in whole or in part, or to refer to it without prior written consent from the office.
While our work included an analysis of financial information, it did not include an audit in accordance with generally accepted auditing standards. The financial information contained in this report has not been subject to examination and confirmation procedures. Therefore, we assume no responsibility and make no undertaking as to the accuracy and completeness of any information received by us, and no confirmation has been made thereof.
The valuation results contained in this report are based on financial information, specific underlying assumptions, and expectations of future events, in the context of market and economic conditions, management decisions, and a review of the financial statements provided to us by the management of Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> However, because events and circumstances may not occur as expected, there will usually be differences between the projected and actual results, and those differences may be material. Accordingly, we do not express an opinion on the conformity of actual results with what is expected, and we do not assume any responsibility or accept any liability of any kind for the achievement of the expected results.

W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023 (hereinafter referred to as "the Company") in accordance with Case No. 159/2023 Sales / 3.

### 1.3. Procedures:
On January 18, 2024, Ms. Rabia Saad Al-Muhanna <orig>رابعه سعد المهنا</orig>, a licensed Class A auditor, license No. 152, appeared before the honorable court and took an oath. ### 1.4. Subject of Valuation
The subject of the valuation is to estimate the fair value of the share owned by Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023.

### 1.5. About the Company and Business Activity
Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> was established under articles of incorporation notarized by the Notary Public, No. 19508, Volume 1, dated June 8, 1976, and as amended by subsequent contracts, including an amendment to the limited liability company contract dated July 9, 2019, which set the company's capital at an amount of 60,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, divided into 100 shares, each valued at 600 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, distributed among the partners as follows:

The purposes for which the company was established are general trading and contracting, buying and selling stocks and bonds for the company's account only, and buying and selling land and real estate for the company's account only.

### 1.6. Standard of Value
The standard of value used is Fair Market Value, which is defined as "the price at which property would change hands between a willing buyer and a willing seller, neither being under any compulsion to buy or to sell and both having reasonable knowledge of relevant facts."

### 1.7. Professional Standards
This valuation and the present report have been prepared in accordance with the professional standards of the National Association of Certified Valuation Analysts (NACVA), where appropriate procedures (in our professional opinion) have been followed to meet the requirements of the scope of work within the time available to complete the valuation report assignment.

### 1.8. Date of Valuation
The valuation was conducted as of December 31, 2023.

### 1.9. Conclusion of Value
In our opinion, based on our analysis of the information presented in this report, the underlying assumptions, and using the net asset value method, the net asset value as of December 31, 2023, has been concluded. Accordingly, the fair value of the equity in Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023, is estimated at 7,294,211 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seven million, two hundred ninety-four thousand, two hundred and eleven Kuwaiti Dinars).

Consequently, the value of a single share is estimated at 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seventy-two thousand, nine hundred forty-two Kuwaiti Dinars and eleven fils) = 7,294,211 ÷ 100 = 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
Upon reviewing the case documents and the documents submitted by Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting (W.L.L.), including the amendment to the limited liability company contract dated July 9, 2019, it is clear to us that the share of Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> consists of one share, representing 1% of the total shares of the company.
The fair market value of the share of Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023, is an amount of 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seventy-two thousand, nine hundred forty-two Kuwaiti Dinars and eleven fils).
It is necessary to draw attention to the following:
a) There is a debit balance due from Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in the amount of 1,341,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, according to the company's data received, listed under the related party receivables balance as of December 31, 2023.
b) According to the documents reviewed, submitted by the management of Mahmoud Haider and Sons for General Trading and Contracting W.L.L., a document dated December 27, 2020, was reviewed, which is a contract for the dissolution of a limited liability company pursuant to an appellate court ruling. The legal opinion issued by the Minister of Justice <orig>وزير العدل</orig> on June 14, 2022, was adopted, under which the share of Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> was amended, making him the owner of 33 shares instead of one share. Accordingly, if this amendment is taken into account, the total value of those 33 shares would be 2,407,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (two million, four hundred seven thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinars and sixty-three fils). Consequently, the net amount due to Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> would be 1,066,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one million, sixty-six thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinars and sixty-three fils) after deducting the debit balance due from him as of December 31, 2023.
In accordance with the court's decision regarding the appointment of the expert dated November 23, 2023, which was to estimate the value of only one share, we have valued the company and determined the value of the single share for Mr. Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haider Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig>. The matter is left to the court to consider the other documents and issued rulings.
This valuation is subject to assumptions and limiting conditions presented in the attached sections of this report. The valuation summary should be read in conjunction with the detailed valuation report presented in the following pages.

# 5. Approaches / Valuation Methods
## 5.1 Valuation Approaches
- There are three traditional valuation approaches: the Income Approach, the Market Approach, and the Cost or Asset Approach. Professionals may differ on the classification or definition of valuation methods within these three types. However, it is generally agreed that all valuation methods can be described as one of these approaches, or a combination of two or more of them.
### 5.1.1 Income Approach
- The Income Approach is based on the economic principle of expectation. In this approach, the value of the investment being valued is the present value of the economic income expected to be generated by the investment. For valuation purposes, the measure of economic income being analyzed can be defined in several ways.
### 5.1.2. Market Approach
- The Market Approach is a method of determining an indication of the value of a business, an ownership interest in a business, a security, or an intangible asset by using one or more methods that compare the subject to similar businesses, ownership interests, securities, or intangible assets that have been sold. Generally, this can be accomplished by comparison with publicly traded companies or by analyzing an actual transaction of a similar sold business. It may also include analyzing previous transactions in the company's shares (if any).
### 5.1.3 Asset Approach
- The Asset Approach is based on the value of net assets less liabilities. As commonly used, this approach begins with the balance sheet book values as of the nearest possible date to the valuation date, and the assets and liabilities, including unrecorded ones, are restated to fair value.
Different valuation methods involving one or more of the three valuation approach categories may be used in any valuation study. All applicable methods must be considered, and the most proven method or methods for valuing the subject property and appropriate for the valuation study should be selected.
## 5.2 The Selected Approach/Method
- The following valuation approach we have adopted to determine the fair value of the equity in the company is the Asset Approach (Net Asset Value Method). This is because Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> has no current operating elements, and its value lies in its net assets and current investments.
## 5.3 Asset Approach (Net Asset Value Method)
- The fair value of the equity in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> has been determined using the Net Asset Value method under the Asset Approach, detailed as follows:
! Analysis of the unaudited management financial statements of the company for the year 2023.
!! Comparison of the book values of tangible assets with the adjusted values.
!!! Classification of the net asset value in a table.

<table_caption>Calculation of Final Equity Value as of December 31, 2023 (Repeated)</table_caption>
<table>
| Value (Kuwaiti Dinar) | Item |
|:---:|:---|
| 8,581,424 | Net Asset Value as of December 31, 2023 |
| (1,287,213) | Less: Lack of marketability discount, risk premium, and pending litigation factor at a rate of 15% |
| 7,294,211 | Final Equity Value as of December 31, 2023 |
</table>

# Notes
1- This represents the outstanding balances of trade debtors, which have been reduced by 50% as a precautionary measure due to substantial doubt about the company's ability to collect these balances, given the lack of current activity.
2- The value of real estate investments has been reduced by 30% due to the inability to determine the market value of these investments.
3- The value of available-for-sale financial investments has been reduced by 50% due to the inability to determine the market value of these investments.
# 6. Conclusion
- Based on our analysis of the information presented in this report, the underlying assumptions, and using the Net Asset Value method, the net asset value as of December 31, 2023, has been determined. Consequently, the fair value of the equity in Mahmoud Haider and Sons General Trading and Contracting Co. W.L.L. <orig>شركة محمود حيدر وأولاده للتجارة العامة والمقاولات ذ.م.م.</orig> as of December 31, 2023, is estimated to be 8,581,424 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Eight million, five hundred eighty-one thousand, four hundred and twenty-four Kuwaiti Dinars). After applying a discount factor of 15%, the value becomes 7,294,211 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Seven million, two hundred ninety-four thousand, two hundred and eleven Kuwaiti Dinars).
- Therefore, the value of a single share is estimated at 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, two

11 Kuwaiti Dinar <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.

- After reviewing the case file and the documents submitted by Mahmoud Haidar & Sons General Trading and Contracting Company (W.L.L.), including an amendment contract for a limited liability company dated July 9, 2019, it is clear to us that the share of Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haidar & Sons General Trading and Contracting Company W.L.L. consists of one share, representing 1% of the total shares of the company.
- The fair market value of the share of Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in Mahmoud Haidar & Sons General Trading and Contracting Company W.L.L., as of December 31, 2023, is an amount of 72,942.11 Kuwaiti Dinar <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (seventy-two thousand nine hundred forty-two Kuwaiti Dinar and eleven fils).

It is necessary to draw attention to the following:
1. There is an outstanding debit balance owed by Mr. / Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> in the amount of 1,341,000 Kuwaiti Dinar <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, according to the data received from the company, listed under the related parties' debit balance as of December 31, 2023.
2. b) According to the documents reviewed, submitted by the management of Mahmoud Haidar & Sons General Trading and Contracting Company W.L.L., a document dated December 27, 2020, was reviewed, which is a contract for the dissolution of a limited liability company pursuant to an appellate court ruling. The legal opinion issued by the Minister of Justice <orig>وزير العدل</orig> on June 14, 2022, was adopted, under which the share of Mr. / Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> was amended, making him the owner of 33 shares instead of one share. Accordingly, if this amendment is taken into account, the total value of those 33 shares would be 2,407,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinar <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (two million, four hundred seven thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinar and sixty-three fils). Consequently, the net amount due to Mr. / Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig> becomes 1,066,089.63 Kuwaiti Dinar <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one million, sixty-six thousand, eighty-nine Kuwaiti Dinar and sixty-three fils) after deducting the outstanding debit balance owed by him as of December 31, 2023.
- In accordance with the court's decision to appoint the expert, dated November 23, 2023, which is to estimate the value of only one share, we have valued the company and determined the value of the single share of Mr. / Maitham Mahmoud Haji Haidar Abdullah <orig>ميثم محمود حاجي حيدر عبد الله</orig>. The matter is left to the court to consider the other submitted documents and rulings.

1. ## Announcement of Public Auction of a Property

The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance announces the public auction of the property described below on Wednesday, 9/7/2025, at 9:00 AM in Hall 5, on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice, in execution of the court's judgment issued in Case No. 198/2024 Sales/2

**Filed by:** Abdulrahman Khaled Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>عبدالرحمن خالد عبدالرحمن احمد الفرحان</orig>.
**Against:** The heirs of the late Sheikha Saleh Abdulaziz Al-Duwaisan <orig>شيخه صالح عبدالعزيز الدويسان</orig>.
The heirs of the late Abdulrahman Ahmed Abdullah Al-Farhan <orig>عبدالرحمن أحمد عبدالله الفرحان</orig>, who are:
1- Fahad Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>فهد عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
2- Tariq Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>طارق عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
3- Sami Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>سامي عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
4- Kholoud Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>خلود عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
5- Laila Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>ليلى عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
6- Rajaa Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>رجاء عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.
7- Sabeeha Abdulrahman Ahmed Al-Farhan <orig>صبيحه عبدالرحمن أحمد الفرحان</orig>.

**First: Property Description: As stated in the Municipality's description certificate.**
The property under Document No. 11844/1999, located in the Hateen <orig>حطين</orig> area – Plot No. 541 <orig>قسيمة رقم 541</orig> – Block No. 3 <orig>قطعة رقم 3</orig> – from Plan No. M/32904, with an area of 437.5 m², will be sold at public auction with a starting price of (620,000 KWD) six hundred and twenty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
** A violation was noted on the property, which is a construction addition on the roof of the first floor.
** According to the attached expert's report – session of 4/9/2023, upon visiting and inspecting the disputed property located in the Hateen <orig>حطين</orig> area – Block (3) – Street No. (311) – Plot (541) – House No. (24), in the presence and guidance of the plaintiff and in the presence of Mr. Sami Al-Tarawneh <orig>سامي الطراورة</orig>, the department's technical expert, while the rest of the litigants were absent. The inspection was carried out as follows:
The property in question is a private residence overlooking a main street, "Subaih Barrak Al-Subaih <orig>صبيح براك الصبيح</orig>," opposite the Al-Shuhada <orig>الشهداء</orig> area, with an area of 437.5m² (according to Document No. 11844/1999). It has one entrance, a setback in front, and is bordered by neighbors on the right, left, and rear.
– The property in question consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a yard (Housh <orig>حوش</orig>).
– The door was knocked, but no one answered. The plaintiff described the property's components from the outside, stating that the ground floor consists of a hall, a small hall, two (2) bedrooms, two (2) bathrooms, a main kitchen, and a maid's room with its bathroom. The exterior cladding is Sigma. There is an elevator and central air conditioning. He was unable to guide the expert on the remaining components of the property.
– The plaintiff stated that the property was previously occupied by the decedents of the parties to the lawsuit (the plaintiff's grandfather and grandmother). The expert determined from the inspection that the property is currently unoccupied.
We, along with the technical expert, inspected the property from the outside, and the technical expert recorded the property's details.

**Second: Auction Conditions:**
First: The auction shall begin at the starting price indicated for the property. To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of that price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department at the Ministry of Justice.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session offering to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 KWD, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, and the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance bears no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges having inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

**Disclaimer:**
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance

The expert found that there are 9 units on the ground floor and 4 on the first floor.
The technical expert inspected the property and reviewed its specifications in preparation for estimating its market value.

- The property has central air conditioning.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at a base price of KWD 670,680 (six hundred seventy thousand, six hundred and eighty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be ruled in their favor, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.

In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder will be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.

# Announcement of Public Auction for a Property
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 10/7/2025 – Hall 5 – on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court ruling issued in Case No. 486/2024 Sales/3, filed by: Intisar Haji Ali Sizali <orig>انتصار حاجي على سيزالى</orig>.
Against:
1- Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Qailani <orig>عبدالله على عبدالله القيلاني</orig>.
2- The Director of the Department of Real Estate Registration and Authentication <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.
3- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.

## Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
Property under Title Deed No. 17425/1995, located in Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig>, Block 2 – Plot No. (7), Parcel No. (5) of Plan No. 36953/M, with an area of 400 m2.
* **Violations exist:**
1- Installation of an unlicensed elevator.
2- There are lightweight Kirby materials on the first floor on the street side of the property, which violates the plan.
* **Inspection:**
The disputed property is located in the Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> area – Block 5 – Street 7 – Plot No. 7 – House No. 35, PACI No.: 132699818. The inspection was conducted as follows:
The disputed property has an area of 400 square meters, according to Title Deed No. 17425/1995, submitted in the plaintiff's document portfolio during the session of 16/1/2024, document No. 2.
The disputed property is a private residence of medium construction, with front and back access, and is bordered by two neighbors on two sides.
The disputed property consists of a ground floor and a first floor.
At the time of inspection, it was found that a second floor, a half third floor, and an elevator shaft have been added, with access from one side of the house. These additions are in the structural frame (black skeleton) phase.
The ground floor consists of a hall with washbasins and a bathroom, another hall with washbasins and a bathroom, a master bedroom with a bathroom, a main kitchen, and a servant's room with a bathroom.
The first floor consists of a hall with a balcony, a kitchenette, and another master bedroom with a bathroom separated by a door. The right side consists of two rooms and a bathroom, and the left side consists of a master bedroom with a bathroom and another room.
The exterior cladding is rough-cut Jordanian stone.
The air conditioning for the ground floor halls is central, while the rest of the floor has split units. The first floor has split units.
The flooring in one hall on the ground floor is marble, and the rest of the property's flooring is ceramic.
The appointed expert has inspected the property and stated that he can estimate the property's value and determine the base price for its sale by public auction and submit a report on the matter.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at a base price of KWD 333,000 (three hundred thirty-three thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of this price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit one-fifth of the price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures. The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> shall bear no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges having inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

Vice President of the Court of First Instance <orig>نائب رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

15- Ebtehal Khalifa Mohammed Al-Jalahma <orig>ابتهال خليفه محمد الجلاهمه</orig>.
16- Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice for Real Estate Registration <orig>وكيل وزارة العدل للتسجيل العقاري</orig>, in his capacity.

**First: Property Description:** In accordance with the attached description certificate.
- A share of 14.432% of the property under Document No. 2018/10501, located in Al-Fahaheel <orig>الفحيحيل</orig> – Block No. 112 – Plot 8 – from Plan No. M/26897 – with an area of 600 m², for a base price of KWD 43,252.704 (Forty-three thousand two hundred fifty-two Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and seven hundred four fils).

***Inspection:***
In a session on 5/2/2024, the disputed property was visited and inspected on-site in the presence and under the guidance of the plaintiff's representative, and in the absence of the other parties despite their proper notification. With the assistance of the Appraisal Expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig>, the inspection was conducted as follows:
- The disputed property is located in the Al-Fahaheel <orig>الفحيحيل</orig> area, Block 10, Street 12, Plot 11208, Building 40, PACI No. 13784377.
- The disputed property is a government house consisting of two and a half stories, located on a single street.
- The exterior cladding of the property is beige Sigma.
- We were unable to enter and inspect the property from the inside.
- The Appraisal Expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> estimated the total value of the disputed property through an external inspection, taking into account the location and condition of the disputed property at the time of inspection.

**Second: Auction Conditions:**
**First:** The auction shall begin at the base price corresponding to the aforementioned share. To participate in the auction, a payment of at least one-fifth of that price is required by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
**Second:** The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
**Third:** If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be repeated at his expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
**Fourth:** If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding is repeated in the same session on the basis of this new price.
**Fifth:** If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately repeated at his expense based on the price that was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
**Sixth:** The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
**Seventh:** This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
**Eighth:** The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
**Note:**
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award ruling is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draft a lease contract in his favor for a similar rent."

Deputy President of the Court of First Instance

# Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 10/7/2025, in Hall 5 on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2023/543 Sales/3.
Filed by: Emad Taha Mohammed Al-Failakawi <orig>عماد طه محمد الفيلكاوي</orig>.
Against:
12- Hassan Qassim Mohammed Hajiyeh <orig>حسن قاسم محمد حاجيه</orig>.
13- The Director General of the Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان</orig>.
First: Property Description: According to the attached Certificate of Description.
- The property under Title Deed No. 2021/15023, located in Sabah Al-Ahmad Residential City <orig>مدينة صباح الأحمد السكنية</orig> – Plot 165 – Block 3 – from Plan No. M/39217 – with an area of 600 m².
*Inspection:*
On 25/6/2024, the expert proceeded to the property subject of the lawsuit, located in the Sabah Al-Ahmad Residential Area <orig>منطقة صباح الأحمد السكنية</orig>, Block 3 – Street 325 – Plot 165 – House 31 – Automated No. 20967278 – from Plan No. M/39217. The inspection was conducted in the presence and with the guidance of the first defendant in person. The plaintiff and the second defendant failed to attend despite being duly notified and aware of the inspection appointment. Mr. Faisal Abdulmohsen Al-Sharhan <orig>فيصل عبد المحسن الشرهان</orig>, the Appointed Expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> retained by the department, was also present. The inspection was carried out as follows:
1- The property in dispute is a private residence with an area of 600 m², as stated in Title Deed No. 2021/15023.
2- The property in dispute consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a room and a storage area on the roof. It is located on a single street, bordered by a neighbor on the right and a neighbor on the left.
3- The exterior cladding of the property is Sigma, beige in color.
4- The air conditioning system in the property is central air conditioning.
5- The ground floor consists of 2 open-plan reception halls, a dining room, 2 bedrooms, 2 bathrooms, a kitchen, and a maid's room with an attached bathroom. In the yard, there is a Diwaniya with an attached bathroom and a guard's room with an attached bathroom.
6- The first floor consists of a hall, 5 bedrooms, and 3 bathrooms.
7- The roof consists of a machine room and a storage area.

# Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 10/7/2025, in Hall 5 on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00

Second: The property under Document No. 2019/8359, located in Hawalli <orig>حولي</orig> – Plot No. 45 – Parcel 19 – from Plan No. M/19263 – with an area of 763 m², to be sold at public auction with a base price of KWD 1,000,000 (one million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>مليون دينار كويتي</orig>).
Note: There are two violations: 1- There is an extension on the ground floor. 2- The third-floor balcony has been enclosed with light materials.
According to what is stated in the description certificate,
The expert visited the properties subject of the dispute, located in the Hawalli <orig>حولي</orig> area, on 8/5/2017, with the assistance of the knowledgeable expert, Mr. Khaled Al-Khodair <orig>خالد الخضير</orig>, and under the guidance of the plaintiffs' agent and their authorized representative, to inspect the properties in preparation for estimating their value. The inspection was carried out as follows:

### First Property:
An investment building located in the Hawalli <orig>حولي</orig> area, Plot 145, Parcel 4, Street 16, branching from Ibn Khaldun <orig>ابن خلدون</orig> Street. Its area is 912 m². The building's condition is old, with standard air conditioning. The building's facades are made of limestone with paint, and it does not have an elevator. The building consists of a ground floor, first floor, second floor, and a roof. It became apparent to the expert that the apartments are occupied and used by others, and she was unable to inspect them from the inside. The representative of the plaintiffs stated that the components of the property are as follows:
- Ground Floor: Contains an annex consisting of three rooms in addition to a separate steam room used as a laundry, and it also contains four apartments.
- First Floor: Contains four apartments.
- Second Floor: Contains four apartments. Roof: Unused.
The property conforms to the general and special specifications stated in Document No. 719 of the year 1971.
Accordingly, the knowledgeable expert inspected the property and recorded his observations in preparation for estimating the property's value.

### Second Property:
An investment building located in the Hawalli <orig>حولي</orig> area, Plot 45, Parcel 19, Street 314. It is situated on a corner and has an area of 763 square meters. The building's condition is medium to old, with standard air conditioning. The facade units are made of limestone with brown porcelain. It contains a non-functional elevator and consists of a ground floor, three repeated floors, and a roof.
It became apparent to the expert that the apartments are occupied and used by others, and the expert was unable to inspect them from the inside. The representative of the plaintiffs stated that the components of the property are as follows:
- Ground Floor: Contains two annexes, each containing two rooms and a living room, in addition to a guard's room.
- The Three Repeated Floors: Each floor contains two large apartments consisting of two rooms and a living room, in addition to two small apartments consisting of one room and a living room.
- Roof: Unused.
The property conforms to the general and special specifications stated in Document No. 3181 of the year 1975.
Accordingly, the knowledgeable expert inspected the property and recorded his observations in preparation for estimating the property's value.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price indicated for the property. To participate in the auction, a payment of at least one-fifth of that price is required by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. The parties initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

The property under Document No. 1994/7140, located in the Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> area, Mubarak Al-Kabeer <orig>مبارك الكبير</orig> Governorate–
