k) Three hundred and twenty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
** As stated in the description certificate:
Automated Address (Al-Qusour <orig>القصور</orig> – Block 6 – Plot 184 of Plan M/36942).
The property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor + first floor + second floor.
The property has an attachment violation on the service road side and with the neighbor, and a violation report No. 3615 has been issued.
** And according to the expert's report:
On 26/3/2024, the expert went to inspect the property subject of the lawsuit, located in the Al-Qusour <orig>القصور</orig> area, Block 6, Street 4, Plot No. 184, House 47, in the presence and under the guidance of the first plaintiff and the fifth and sixth defendants. The due diligence expert, retained by the administration, also attended to inspect the property subject of the lawsuit in preparation for estimating its value and the value of its yield/usufruct. After examination and inspection, the expert found the following:

### General Description of the Disputed Property
The property subject of the lawsuit is located in the Al-Qusour <orig>القصور</orig> area, Block 6, Street 4, Plot No. 184, House 47. The property is situated on a single street, bordered by neighbors on both sides, with an alleyway at the back and a setback consisting of parking for 6 cars. The exterior cladding of the disputed property is white Sigma paint. The property consists of a ground floor, first floor, second floor, and a roof. It has 3 main iron entrances, an elevator, and is fully equipped with split-unit air conditioning.

### Specific Description of the Disputed Property
Under the guidance of the fifth and sixth defendants, the expert inspected the interior of the property. The ground floor consists of 3 reception halls, a diwaniya, a storeroom, a room, two bathrooms, a maid's room with its bathroom, and a main kitchen. The first floor is composed of two parts. The fifth defendant stated that the first part of the first floor consists of 3 rooms and a bathroom, and this part is used by the first and ninth defendants and the second plaintiff, but the second plaintiff moved out approximately a year ago. As for the second part of the first floor, the expert knocked on the door, and the eighth defendant responded and allowed the expert to inspect the part he occupies, which consists of a hall, two bathrooms, a bedroom, a dressing room, a kitchen, a laundry room, and an attached bathroom. The second floor is also composed of two parts. The first part belongs to the sixth defendant and consists of two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen. As for the second part of the second floor, the expert knocked on the door, and the seventh defendant responded and showed the part he occupies, which consists of a hall, a kitchen, two rooms, and two bathrooms. The fifth defendant stated that he, the second, third, and fourth defendants, and the first plaintiff do not occupy the property. The due diligence expert recorded the general and specific descriptions of the property in preparation for estimating its value and the value of its yield/usufruct.

### Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price indicated for the property. To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of that price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless another person comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures and under their responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Public Auction for the Sale of a Property
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 10/7/2025, in Hall 5 on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court ruling issued in Case No. 772/2023 Sales/3.
Filed by: Khalid Rashid Mohammed Al-Gharibah <orig>خالد راشد محمد الغريبه</orig>.
Against:
1- Khalida Rashid Mohammed Al-Gharibah <orig>خالده رشيد محمد الغريبه</orig>.
2- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>
First: Description of the property according to the attached description certificate.
Property under Title Deed No. 2010/8902, located in Abdullah Al-Mubarak Suburb <orig>ضاحية عبدالله المبارك</orig> – Block No. 5 – Plot 183 – Plan M/38235 – with an area of 400 m2.
Note: There is a violation report for an additional construction on the roof measuring 25 m2.
According to the description certificate,
On 26/7/2023, the expert went to the disputed property in the Abdullah Mubarak Al-Sabah <orig>عبد الله مبارك الصباح</orig> area – Block 5, Block 5 – Street 508 – House 3 – Plot 183 – Automated No. 16258049 – with an area of 400 m2,
in the presence of the due diligence expert, Mr. Abdulrahman Al-Habib <orig>عبد الرحمن الحبيب</orig>, and under the personal guidance of the defendant, while the plaintiff failed to attend. The expert was enabled to enter the house at the time of inspection as follows:-
1- The disputed property is a private residence on a corner lot, bordered by neighbors on two sides. It has 4 entrances: two main entrances leading to the ground floor, a third entrance leading to the diwaniya, the kitchen, and the stairs to the rented second floor, and a fourth entrance leading to the kitchen.
2- The disputed property consists of a ground floor, first floor, second floor, and a roof. The exterior cladding is beige Sigma paint, and the house has central air conditioning. The property contains

3- The ground floor consists of 2 halls, 2 washbasins, a bathroom, a master bedroom, a main kitchen, a diwaniya, a driver's room, and a bathroom.

a- The first apartment consists of 2 bedrooms, 2 bathrooms, a hall, and a preparatory kitchen.
b- The second apartment consists of 3 bedrooms, 2 bathrooms, a hall, and a preparatory kitchen.

7- The Appraisal Expert <orig>خبير الدراسة</orig> inspected the property in preparation for estimating its current market value and submitting the relevant report.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at a base price of 387,000 K.D. (three hundred eighty-seven thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of this price by a certified check from the drawee bank or a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, in addition to expenses and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability during the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the person whose bid was approved deposits at least one-fifth of the price, the sale shall be postponed with a one-tenth increase.
Fifth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless another person comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a one-tenth increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction shall be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Sixth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the one-tenth increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at their liability based on the price at which it was previously awarded to them. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Seventh: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Eighth: This announcement is published in application of the law. The parties initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Ninth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."

Vice President of the Court of First Instance <orig>نائب رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Public Auction for the Sale of a Property
The Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 10/7/2025, in Hall 5 on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2022/775 Sales/3
Filed by:
1- Afrah Hamad Abdulsayyed Al-Shatti <orig>افراح حمد عبدالسيد الشطي</orig>, on her own behalf and in her capacity as custodian and guardian of her son Abdulrahman Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عبدالرحمن راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
2- Yousef Rashed Othman Abdullah Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>يوسف راشد عثمان عبدالله عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
3- Fiddah Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>فضة راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
4- Moudhi Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>موضي راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
Against:
1- Aisha Salem Abdullah Bughaith <orig>عائشة سالم عبدالله بوغيث</orig>.
2- Rasha Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>رشا راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
3- Rana Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>رنا راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
4- Bodour Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>بدور راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
5- Abdullah Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عبدالله راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
6- Othman Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عثمان راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
7- Hamad Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>حمد راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
8- Director of the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>مدير إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>, in his capacity.
9- Zahra Khidr Ali Al-Fares <orig>زهرة خضر علي الفارس</orig>
First: Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
- Property under Document No. (14237/1997) located in the suburb of Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> – Block No. (8), Plot No. (2) of Plan No. (M/36984), with an area of (300.325 m2), taking into account the right of residence for the divorcée Zahra Khidr Ali Al-Fares <orig>زهرة خضر على الفارس</orig> until the end of the children's custody period, according to the letter from the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>.
Note:
There is a violation, which is a room built on the roof, according to the Municipality's letter.
*Inspection:
The property is located in the Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area – Block 8 – Street 1 – Avenue 15 – House – Plot 2, Automated No. 11942204. The inspection was carried out as follows:
- The property in dispute is a government house located on two streets (front and back), an internal street and a main street, and is bordered by two neighbors. It consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof.
- The property has an area of 300 m2 according to the document submitted by the plaintiffs' agent at the session of 13/1/2022. The exterior is finished with Sigma, and it has central and unit air conditioning.
- The property in dispute has two entrances. The first is on the internal street side and is independently used by the plaintiffs. It consists of a portion of the ground floor, which includes a diwaniya + bathroom and washbasins + four (4) rooms + three (3) bathrooms + a living hall + a kitchen.
- As for the second entrance on the main street side, the door was knocked on several times, but no one answered. The plaintiffs' agent stated that this part is independently used by the defendant and Ms. Zahra Khidr Al-Fares <orig>زهراء خضر الفارس</orig> (the decedent's ex-wife and mother of the second to seventh defendants). Therefore, he cannot enable the expert to inspect this part, explaining that it consists of: a kitchen on the ground floor, the entire first floor, and the roof.
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction will start at a base price of 317,115 K.D. (Three hundred seventeen thousand, one hundred fifteen Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of this price is required, either by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the auction session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at his own risk during the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless another person comes forward in this session offering to purchase with an increase of one-tenth, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the one-tenth increase, the auction is immediately reopened at his own risk on the basis of the price that was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the price of the property.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., lawyer's and expert's fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to issue a lease contract in his favor for a similar rent."

Vice President of the Court of First Instance <orig>نائب رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Public Auction for the Sale of a Property
The Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below on Tuesday, 13/7/2025, in Hall 5 on the eighth floor of the New Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2024/828 Sales/4
Filed by:
Heirs of the late Abdullah Mushailih Al-Marzouq <orig>عبدالله مشيلح المرزوق</orig>, who are: 1- Fakhriya Kshaish Hamad <orig>فخرية كشيش حمد</orig>.
<page_end>71</page_end>

**First: Description of the property according to the attached description certificate:**
The property of Document No. 4161/1966, located in the Al-Shamiya <orig>الشامية</orig> area, Plot No. 74, Block No. 7, Model 3 of Plan M/8-2/2-1, with an area of 750 m², to be sold by public auction at a base price of KWD 1,450,000 (one million, four hundred and fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
**The description certificate states:**
The property consists of a ground floor and a first floor as of the date of inspection.
**And according to the expert's report:**
In a session on 26/10/2023, we proceeded to the disputed property located in the Al-Shamiya <orig>الشامية</orig> area, Block 7 - Jassim Hamad Al-Saqr Street - Plot No. 74 - House 35 - PACI No. 10402046, in the presence and under the guidance of the thirteenth plaintiff from the 'First' section in person. The remaining plaintiffs and all defendants were absent despite being notified of the scheduled date. Also present from the administration was the consulting study expert, Mr. Faisal Abdul Mohsen Al-Sharhan <orig>فيصل عبد المحسن الشرهان</orig>. The inspection was conducted as follows:
1. The disputed property conforms in its general and specific specifications to Document No. (4161/1966) and has an area of 750 m² pursuant to a sales contract issued by the Government of Kuwait, submitted in the plaintiffs' document portfolio dated 18/10/2023, document No. 13.
2- The disputed property is a house overlooking one street and is bordered by neighbors on

3. The property subject to the dispute is very old, as the appointed expert reported that it is dilapidated.
4. The property subject to the dispute consists of a ground floor and a roof, with the following details:
The ground floor consists of (7) rooms + (2) bathrooms + a kitchen + an open courtyard.
The roof consists of (2) rooms + a bathroom.
5. There is no air conditioning in the house.
6. The exterior cladding of the property is painted cement plaster, parts of which are falling off.
7. The property was unoccupied at the time of inspection, as it is abandoned and the windows are without glass.
8. We took photographs of the disputed property.
9. The appointed expert, assigned by the administration, inspected the property in preparation for estimating its value, determining the base price for the property, and submitting the relevant report.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price indicated for the property. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction shall be repeated at his own risk during the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, a judgment shall be issued awarding the auction to him, unless another person comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with an increase of one-tenth, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction shall be repeated in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the one-tenth increase, the auction shall be immediately repeated at his own risk based on the price that had been awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures, and under their responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
4- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in his favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance

Automated Case No.: 220361040

Nationality: Egypt Civil ID No.: 270021902329
issued an in-absentia judgment ruling: To fine the defendant the sum of one hundred Kuwaiti Dinars for the charge against him.
The Public Prosecution hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to execute it in accordance with the provisions of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials <orig>قانون الإجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>. It should be noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through opposition or appeal, the judgment shall become final and enforceable against him.

### Announcement of a Penal Judgment
The Misdemeanors Court, in its session held on 13-10-2021,
In Case No.: 20/004088 - Commercial Affairs Prosecution, Commercial Misdemeanors
Police Station No.: (20/0008370 - Public Authority for Food) -
Automated Case No.: 201201570
Against the defendant: Sulaiman Mohammed Nazirullah Mohammed <orig>سلیمان محمد نظیرالله محمد</orig>
Nationality: India

## Announcement of a Criminal Judgment
The Court of First Instance, in its session held on 11-08-2021,
in Case No.: 21/008420 - Court of First Instance, Municipal Misdemeanors and Violations
Police Station No.: (19/0004889 - Municipality)
Automated Case No.: 211793060
Against the accused: Govindaraj Subramani <orig>جوفيندراج – سوبراماني</orig>
Nationality: India
Civil ID No.: 276021017634
issued a judgment in absentia stipulating:
A fine of one hundred dinars to be imposed on the accused for the charges attributed to him. The Public Prosecution hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and directs all security authorities to execute it in accordance with the provisions of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through an opposition or appeal, the judgment shall become final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution <orig>مدير نيابة التنفيذ الجنائي</orig>

## Announcement of a Criminal Judgment
The Court of First Instance, in its session held on 07-11-2021,
in Case No. 002153 / 21 - Court of First Instance, ordinary misdemeanors
Police Station No.: ( 0001106 / 16 - Jleeb Al-Shuyoukh <orig>جليب الشيوخ</orig> ) -
Automated Case No.: 200769540
Against the accused: Rakesh Kumar Raj <orig>راكش كومار راج</orig>
Nationality: India, Civil ID No.: 289111105374
issued a judgment in absentia, ruling:
To imprison the accused for one month with labor and enforcement, and to deport him from the country after the execution of the sentence.
The Public Prosecution hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to execute it in accordance with the provisions of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through an opposition or appeal, the judgment shall become final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution

### Announcement of a Criminal Judgment
The Misdemeanor Court, in its session held on 13-12-2021,
in Case No.: 21/000711 - Media and Information Technology Prosecution
Police Station No.: (21/0000585 - Misdemeanors Investigations)
Automated Case No.: 211008300
Against the defendant: Abdul Rahman Hamad Alwan Al-Owais <orig>عبد الرحمن حمد علوان العويص</orig>
Nationality: Syria
Civil ID No.: 293110501203
issued a judgment in absentia, ruling:
To imprison the defendant for a period of six months with labor and enforcement for the charge attributed to him due to connection, to refer the civil case to the competent civil circuit, and for the court clerk's office to set a hearing date and notify the litigants. The Public Prosecution announces this judgment to the convicted person and directs all security authorities to execute it in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person challenging the judgment through opposition or appeal, the judgment will become final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution

---

## Announcement
The following is a necessary addendum to the announcement of the "Annual Plan of the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy for the Fiscal Year (2025-2026)," published in the Official Gazette "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>" in issue number (1741) dated 01/06/2025.

First: Electricity Distribution Networks Sector

# Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>
## Announcement of Sale by Sealed-Bid Auction, Auction No. (2472)
The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of computers and their accessories, office furniture, office equipment, iron, wires, and other various out-of-service materials by sealed-bid auction at the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig> according to the following details:
1.  Location for receiving the terms booklet and auction participation offer: Sharq - Headquarters of the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig> - Financial Affairs Department - Cashier's Office, from 15/6/2025 to 19/6/2025. The documents will be provided for a non-refundable fee of (20) Dinars, payable to the cashier of the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>. Upon receiving the terms booklet, the bidder will sign a declaration and undertaking to adhere to the specified deadline for submitting the bid to the Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
2.  Inspection Date: (5) working days from 15/6/2025 to 19/6/2025. Inspection Time: During official working hours (from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM).
3.  Location for receiving those wishing to inspect the auction items:
    *   Sharq - Headquarters of the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>.
4.  Date for submitting bids and opening envelopes:
    *   Bids are to be submitted on Sunday, 22/6/2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Warehousing Affairs Department - Central Sales Section, according to the deadline specified for the bidder by the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig> (No bid will be accepted after the bidder's specified deadline has passed).
    *   Envelopes will be opened and the auction held on Monday, 23/6/2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> - Ministries Complex - Block 12 - Third Floor - General Warehousing Affairs Department.
    *   The winning bidder will be announced on the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> website on Monday, 23/6/2025.
    *   Checks will be returned to unsuccessful bidders on Tuesday, 24/6/2025.
    *   The certified check / bank guarantee must be submitted in the name of the Fatwa and Legislation Department <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>.
*   Special Conditions for the Auction:
    *   The bidder (establishment or company) must be Kuwaiti, registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. A foreigner may participate provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or a commercial agent under a notarized contract. To obtain the bid documents, please visit the headquarters of the Ministry of Communications <orig>وزارة المواصلات</orig> in the Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> area – Jamal Abdul Nasser Street <orig>شارع جمال عبدالناصر</orig> – Building No. (2), Third Floor – Procurement and Warehousing Department <orig>إدارة المشتريات والمخازن</orig> – Tenders Supervision <orig>مراقبة المناقصات</orig>, to receive the bid documents booklet during official working hours.
- Bid validity period is (90) days from the date of bid opening. The preliminary insurance value shall be not less than (2%) and not more than (5%) of the bid value, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee from one of the approved local banks in Kuwait, valid for the duration of the bid and issued in the name of the Ministry of Communications <orig>وزارة المواصلات</orig>.
- Companies wishing to participate must adhere to the following:
  1- Provide a letter of authorization from the company to purchase the documents.
  2- Provide a valid clearance certificate <orig>براءة الذمة</orig> for the Ministry.
  3- Provide a clearance certificate <orig>براءة الذمة</orig> document from the Ministry of Electricity, Water, and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>.
  4- Provide the national labor percentage certificate.
  5- Provide a copy of the commercial license.
  6- Provide a copy of registration with the Kuwait Chamber of Industry <orig>غرفة صناعة الكويت</orig>.
  7- Provide a copy of registration with the Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig>.
  8- Provide a copy of the company's articles of association <orig>عقد تأسيس الشركة</orig>.
  9- Provide a tax certificate from the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
  10- Provide a registration certificate from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
  11- Provide a certificate from the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.
Bids shall be deposited in the designated box located at the Tenders and Practices Section headquarters – Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> – Building No. (2), Third Floor, until the end of Thursday, 2025/7/10, at 1:00 PM. All bidders must submit their bids in a sealed envelope with red wax, clearly marked with the bid number and subject.

All bidders must submit their bids in a red wax-sealed envelope, clearly marked with the auction number and subject.

## Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>
### Announcement
Public Practice <orig>الممارسة العامة</orig> No. (D/M/811) Supply, Installation, Operation, Maintenance, and Warranty of an Integrated Wireless Digital Microphone System with a Touch Screen
The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces the issuance of Public Practice <orig>الممارسة العامة</orig> No. (D/M/811) – Supply, Installation, Operation, Maintenance, and Warranty of an Integrated Wireless Digital Microphone System with a Touch Screen. Companies or institutions specialized in this field who wish to participate may obtain the booklet of conditions <orig>كراسة الشروط</orig> and practice documents during official working hours from (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7 – Tenders and Follow-up Department) during official working hours, starting from the date of this announcement's publication in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), for a non-refundable fee of (75/- K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (payment by K-Net only) for the booklet. Owners of small and medium enterprises are exempt from these fees (upon presentation of the relevant certificate). This will be available starting from Sunday, 15/06/2025, from 8:30 AM until 1:00 PM, with the following to be observed:
1- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Sunday, 29/06/2025. No bids will be accepted after this deadline.
2- Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department – at Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
3- Submission of an initial deposit <orig>تأمين أولي</orig> of not less than (2%) of the bid value in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>, in the form of a letter of guarantee <orig>خطاب ضمان</orig> or a certified check <orig>شيك مصدق</orig> from a Kuwaiti bank, valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity, which is (90) days.
4- Submission of a valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage <orig>نسبة العمالة الوطنية</orig>.
5- A letter of authorization and a copy of the Civil ID of the company's representative for purchasing the practice document.
6- This practice is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
7- The practitioner must submit a letter with an attached copy of the registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
8- The preliminary meeting is scheduled for Monday, 23/06/2025, at 11:00 AM, at the Tenders and Follow-up Department – at Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
9- The bid must remain valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date, with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserving the right to extend or renew this period for the duration(s) it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.
The practice is subject to Circular No. (5) of 2020 regarding procurement systems for public entities.
For inquiries:
Contact Mr. Abdulaziz Al-Duwailah <orig>عبدالعزيز الدويلة</orig>

- Email: sa.alhasawi@da.gov.kw

# Announcement
## Regarding Tender No. (D.A/M/805)
## Renewal of SolarWinds Program Licenses for Network Performance Analysis at the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>

The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces the extension of the closing date for Tender No. (D/A/M/805) for the renewal of SolarWinds program licenses for network performance analysis at the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>. Companies or institutions specialized in this field wishing to participate may obtain the booklet of conditions and tender documents during official working hours from (the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7 – Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig>). This is available during official working hours starting from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D. /-) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> (payment via K-Net only) for the booklet. Small and medium enterprises are exempt from this fee (upon presentation of a certificate proving such status). This is available from 8:30 AM to 1:00 PM, taking into account the following:

1- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Thursday, 19/06/2025. No bids will be accepted after this time.
2- Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
3- A preliminary deposit of not less than (1,000 K.D. /-) must be submitted in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from a Kuwaiti bank, valid for the duration of the bid's validity, which is (90) days.
4- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage and a valid tax compliance certificate must be submitted.
5- An authorization letter and a copy of the Civil ID of the company's representative for purchasing the tender document.
6- This tender is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
7- The bidder must submit a letter with an attached copy of the registration certificate from the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
8- The preliminary meeting will be held on Tuesday, 10/06/2025, at 10:30 AM at (the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7 – Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig>). The bid must remain valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date, with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserving the right to extend or renew this period for the duration(s) it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.

# National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig>
## Announcement

The National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig> announces Tender No. M.W.TH.F.A – 8 (2025/2026) for the maintenance of indoor and outdoor plants for the buildings of the National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters.
Specialized companies wishing to participate in this tender may obtain the tender documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> from the Financial Affairs Department – Contracts Section – Second Floor – National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters building – Al-Shuhada Street – Sharq.
The following must be observed:
1- The tender is indivisible, and alternative offers are not accepted.
2- The preliminary meeting to answer inquiries from participating bidders will be held five working days after the date of this announcement's publication in the Official Gazette, at the headquarters of the General Secretariat of the National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters, at 11:00 AM in the ground floor meeting room.
3- The deadline for submitting bids is within (10 working days from the date of this announcement's publication in Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>جريدة الكويت اليوم</orig>).
4- All documents must be submitted on three (3) CDs, with the exception of (the bid form, the preliminary deposit, a copy of the purchase receipt, and the bidder's information form).
5- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend the bid-opening session, after coordinating with the Procurement Monitoring Department (Contracts Section) before the day scheduled for the bid-opening session.

The Secretary-General

- Bidders must adhere to the instructions for submitting bids (on CD) on the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
- Companies/bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must do so at the time and place specified above in the preliminary meeting schedule (inquiry session). No inquiries will be considered after the deadline.
- All documents must be submitted on a CD and a non-reproducible hard copy, with the exception of the bid form and the initial bid bond, which must be submitted as a hard copy.

Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for the purchase of the tender documents, the initial bid bond, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no holds on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority, nor any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. It should be noted that any bid that does not include this certificate will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance of consumption debts.
The tender is open to all companies and institutions specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by the Ministry of Finance circulars), accompanied by the following:-
1- A copy of the tender announcement in the Official Gazette.
2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
3- A written authorization letter, approved by the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID – a copy of the signature authorization).
- Owners of small and medium enterprises are exempt from the fees for purchasing the tender documents, in accordance with the provisions of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to the Public Tenders Law No. (49/2016).
- Owners of small and medium enterprises wishing to apply for the tender must attach to their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise, in accordance with the provisions of Article (48) of the Public Tenders Law No. (49 of 2016 AD), which states, "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session in the presence of the bidders or their representatives."
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend. Companies wishing to attend the bid opening session have the right to coordinate with the competent committee before the day of the session.
- This announcement is an integral part of the tender documents.
Note: The Authority may cancel the tender without stating reasons and without any objection from the bidders.
- For more information, please visit the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw).

Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the closing date, and must be delivered in wax-sealed envelopes.

## Announcement

A preliminary meeting for bidders has been scheduled at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor) at 10:00 AM on Sunday, 22/6/2025. Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the closing date. Bids must be delivered in red wax-sealed envelopes and placed in the designated box for tenders at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor). Any bids received after the specified deadline for the tender closing will not be accepted.
- Bidders must adhere to the instructions for submitting bids (CD) on the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> website (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
- Companies/bidders wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must do so at the time and place specified above for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). No inquiries will be considered after this time.
- All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-reproducible hard copy, with the exception of the bid form and the initial guarantee, which must be submitted as a hard copy. Bids shall be valid for a period of (90) ninety days from the date of bid opening. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for the purchase of the tender documents, the initial guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be disqualified.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no holds on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority, nor any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. It should be noted that any bid that does not include this certificate will be disqualified.
- The bidder must attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> confirming clearance of consumption debts.
- The tender is open to all companies and institutions specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (75 K.D.), only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by the circulars of the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>). The following must be brought along: -
  1- A copy of the tender announcement in the Official Gazette.
  2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
  3- A written authorization letter approved by the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID - a copy of the signature authorization).
- Owners of small and medium enterprises are exempt from the fees for purchasing the tender documents, in accordance with the provisions of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to the Public Tenders Law No. (49/2016).
- Owners of small and medium enterprises wishing to apply for the tender must attach to their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise, in accordance with the provisions of Article (48) of the Public Tenders Law No. (49 of 2016), which states, "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session in the presence of the bidders or their representatives."

---

- This announcement serves as an invitation to interested bidders. Companies wishing to attend the bid opening session have the right to coordinate with the competent committee before the day of the session.
- This announcement is an integral part of the tender documents.
- Note: The Authority may cancel the tender without stating reasons and without any objection from the bidders.
- For more information, please visit the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw).

The Public Authority for Youth <orig>الهيئة العامة للشباب</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. H.A.SH/M.S/7/2025/2026 regarding the organization of sports activities in swimming (Youth Centers: Fun and Enjoyment Project), through sealed envelopes in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents. These documents can be obtained from the Public Authority for Youth <orig>الهيئة العامة للشباب</orig>, located in the Jaber Al-Ahmad area – Jaber Al-Ahmad Youth Center <orig>مركز شباب جابر الأحمد</orig> – Plot (7) – (N3) – Street 60 – First Floor, during official working hours.

Companies and institutions required to participate in this tender may obtain the tender document by submitting a letter expressing their desire to purchase the tender, which must be signed by the person authorized to sign on behalf of the company or institution.
Note that a preliminary meeting for bidders has been scheduled at the administrative building of the Public Authority for Youth <orig>الهيئة العامة للشباب</orig> in the Shuwaikh Industrial Area - First Floor, at twelve o'clock noon on Sunday, 22/6/2025.
Bids must be submitted from nine o'clock in the morning until one o'clock in the afternoon on the closing date. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red wax and placed in the designated box for tenders at the Authority's headquarters at the Jabir Al-Ahmad Youth Center - First Floor. No bids received after the specified deadline for the tender closing will be accepted.
The bidder must ensure that the bid is valid for a period of (90) ninety days from the closing date. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for the purchase of the tender documents, the original preliminary guarantee, and a valid national labor support certificate issued by the Ministry of Social Affairs and Labor <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية والعمل</orig> will be excluded.
This tender is limited to companies and institutions specialized in the required works and registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, provided that the registration certificate is valid.
All bidding companies must have their representative attend the bid-opening meeting at the Public Authority for Youth <orig>الهيئة العامة للشباب</orig> on Thursday, 3/7/2025, at two-thirty in the afternoon.
Note: The Authority may cancel the tender without stating reasons and without any objection from the bidders.
Acting Director General of the Public Authority for Youth <orig>الهيئة العامة للشباب</orig>

# Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig>
## Announcement
### Al-Dibdibah Power Generation Project and Al-Shaqaya Renewable Energy Project – Phase III <orig>مشروع الدبدبة لتوليد الطاقة الكهربائية ومشروع الشقايا للطاقات المتجددة – المرحلة الثالثة</orig>
### Project One – (Zone 1 (PV
The Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig> ("the Authority"), in cooperation with the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> ("the Ministry"), is pleased to invite the qualified investors ("Qualified Investors") announced in the Official Gazette Issue (1700) dated 18/8/2024 and referred to below, to obtain the Request for Proposal (RFP) documents and participate in the bid for the implementation of the Al-Dibdibah Power Generation Project and Al-Shaqaya Renewable Energy Project – Phase III – Project One – (Zone-1) ("the Project") in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (39) of 2010 concerning the establishment of Kuwaiti public joint-stock companies to build and execute electric power and water desalination plants in Kuwait, and its amendments and executive regulations, and Law No. (116) of 2014 concerning Public-Private Partnerships and its executive regulations.

## Qualified Consortia:

### 1- Project Summary:
The Al-Dibdibah Power Generation Project and the Shagaya Renewable Energy Project – Phase III – Project 1 – Zone 1 is a renewable energy plant with a net capacity of 1100 MW. The project will be part of the Shagaya Renewable Energy Park ("SREP") located within the administrative boundaries of the Al-Jahra Governorate <orig>محافظة الجهراء</orig>, west of Kuwait City <orig>مدينة الكويت</orig>, approximately 100 kilometers from the capital.

### 2- Project Objective:
Through this project, the Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects (KAPP) <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig> and the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والمياه والطاقة المتجددة</orig> aim to encourage private sector participation in the country's construction and development projects, due to its positive impact on the local economy, particularly through attracting capital and transferring technology and knowledge. This achieves competition, enhances workforce efficiency, and raises the level of services provided. It also contributes to meeting the country's growing electricity needs, providing the essential infrastructure for implementing other state projects within its development plan, and improving power generation levels to strengthen the existing grid. Additionally, it aims to achieve competition in the electricity sectors and increase the capacity of renewable energy within the national energy mix.

### 3- Investment Period:

# Kuwait Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>
## Announcement
Hiring the services of an in-house employee to translate special documents from English to Arabic for the Kuwait Investment Authority
The Kuwait Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig> announces the opening of registration for specialized local companies and institutions. Applications for registration can be submitted at the Kuwait Investment Authority building – Administrative, Financial, and Personnel Affairs Department, during official working hours starting from Sunday, 15/06/2025. Please note that the deadline for registration is Thursday, 03/07/2025, at 1:00 PM. Applications must be submitted at the Authority's headquarters (Sharq Area <orig>منطقة شرق</orig> – Block 1 – Street 211 – Plot 900028 – 22nd Floor – Office No. 2215) before the closing date.
Companies and institutions wishing to register must meet the following conditions:
1. A copy of the translation accreditation from the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
2. A valid translation license from the Ministry of Information <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>.
3. A certificate of commercial register extract.
4. An authorization letter from the company for registration.
5. The company must be specialized in this field.
6. The company must provide a valid certificate of national labor percentage in non-governmental entities.

  "page_title": "Al Dibdibah Power and Al Shagaya Renewable Energy – Phase III – Zone 1 Solar PV IPP Announcement of Request for Proposal",

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1743, Seventy-First Year
109
Sunday, 19 Dhu al-Hijjah 1446 H – 15/6/2025 G
</header>

The Project Company ("the Generator") must conclude a Power Purchase Agreement ("PPA") with the Ministry, under which it will export its production to the electricity grid in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> for a period of (30) years from the Commercial Operation Date of the Project ("PCOD").

## 4- Contractual Framework:
The agreements include the legal and commercial terms and conditions governing the project's operation, including, for example, the following terms and conditions:
- Development, financing, design, supply, engineering, construction, testing, and operation of the plant and the 400 kV substation for exporting electrical power.
- Ownership, operation, and maintenance of the plant by the Project Company (the Generator).
- The conditions that will govern the process of selling and purchasing electricity between the Project Company (the Generator) and the buyer, and the terms and conditions for payment of installments to the Project Company (the Generator).
- Deductions and compensations payable by the Project Company (the Generator) in the event of a breach of the agreement's terms and conditions, and any other compensations.
- Conditions and procedures for the transfer of the project's assets and employees to the State upon the expiration of the contract term, including the requirements for handing over the assets and the project to the State.
Other agreements will include, but are not limited to (the Undertaking Document, the Substitution Agreement, the Land Lease Agreement for the project site and areas designated for temporary use, and the Shareholders' Agreement for the establishment and management of the Project Company (the Generator)).

## 5- Fee for Obtaining Tender Documents:
Qualified investors wishing to obtain the Request for Proposal documents must sign and submit a confidentiality agreement to the Authority before receiving those documents.
The Authority invites qualified investors to obtain the Request for Proposal documents by paying a fee of KWD 7,000 (seven thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) to the "Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig>" through any of the following payment methods:
(a) Transfer the amount to the Authority's account IBAN (KW07CBKU00000000000000000012012039), taking into account that the transfer value must be net of any fees. The Authority may require confirmation of receipt of the transfer, which may take no less than three (3) business days.
(b) Submit a non-refundable certified check issued by a bank licensed to operate in the State of Kuwait, payable to the "Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig>".
(c) Electronic payment service (K-net) (Visa/Mastercard are not accepted).
For payment methods (b) and (c), interested parties must deliver the payment to:
Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig>
Touristic Enterprises Company Building – Second Floor
Shuwaikh Administrative Area <orig>الشويخ الإدارية</orig> – Jahra Road <orig>شارع الجهراء</orig>
Kuwait
Phone: +965 2496 64/5950
Once the payment process is complete, the applicant must send proof of payment via email to Alshagaya@kapp.gov.kw in order to receive the bidding documents. Note that the deadline for purchasing the bidding documents is September 14, 2025.
Applying companies and consortia must submit their bids in a sealed envelope addressed as follows:
Headquarters of the Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig> located at: Shuwaikh Administrative Area <orig>منطقة الشويخ الإدارية</orig> – Jahra Road <orig>شارع الجهراء</orig> – Touristic Enterprises Company Building – Second Floor.
An envelope marked "Envelope – 1" containing the Technical Proposal and all data and documents mentioned in Clause 7.3 of the Instructions to Bidders document.
An envelope marked "Envelope – 2" containing the Financial Proposal and all data and documents mentioned in Clause 7.3 of the Instructions to Bidders document.
All companies and consortia must submit (1) original printed hard copy of the bids, a second printed hard copy marked as (Copy), and (3) electronic copies marked (FD1) – for the Technical Proposal, (3) electronic copies marked (FD2) for the Financial Proposal, and (3) electronic copies marked (Envelope 1, Envelope 2), with the technical and financial envelopes being separate, no later than 12:00 PM Kuwait time on Sunday, September 14, 2025.
A qualified investor who fails to obtain the bidding documents within the date and period specified in this announcement shall be deemed to have irrevocably waived their right to participate in the project's auction.
For any inquiries, please contact via email: Alshagaya@kapp.gov.kw
This invitation does not in any way obligate the Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects <orig>هيئة مشروعات الشراكة بين القطاعين العام والخاص</orig> to proceed to the next stage or award the bid. The Authority reserves the full right to cancel the project, restart the stage with any amendments it deems appropriate, extend the stage, or continue with the project in another manner at any time without any liability on the part of the Authority or any other government entity.

# Al Dibdibah Power and Al Shagaya Renewable Energy – Phase III – Zone 1 Solar PV IPP Announcement of Request for Proposal
The Bidding Committee of Al Dibdibah Power and Al Shagaya Renewable Energy – Phase III – Zone 1 Solar PV IPP in coordination with Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects (“KAPP”), and the Ministry of Electricity & Water & Renewable Energy (“MEWRE”) in the state of Kuwait ” is pleased to invite the qualified bidders (“Qualified Bidders”) whom are announced in the official Gazette issue No.(1700) dated 18/08/2024 to participate in bidding in the Request for Proposal (“RFP”) of the Al Dibdibah Power and Al Shagaya Renewable Energy – Phase III – Zone 1 Solar PV IPP (the “Project”) in accordance with Law No. 39 of 2010 establishing Kuwaiti joint stock companies to undertake the construction and implementation of electric power and water desalination plants in Kuwait, its amendments and its Executive Regulations, Law (116/2014) and its Executive Regulations.

## Qualified Companies:

<table_caption>Qualified Companies</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Company name |
|---|---|
| 1 | Trung Nam Construction Investment Corp |
| 2 | TotalEnergies Renewables SAS |

## 1- Project Brief:
Al Dibdibah Power and Al Shagaya Renewable Energy – Phase III – Zone 1 Solar PV IPP, is a renewable power plant with a net capacity of 1,100 MW of power. The Project will be part of AlShagaya Renewable Energy Park (“SREP”) located within the administrative boundary of the Jahra Governorate to the West of Kuwait City, approximately 100 kilometers from the capital city.

## 2- Project Objective:
Through the launch of this Project, the Public-Private Partnership Projects Authority and the Ministry of Electricity & Water & Renewable Energy aim to encourage the private sector to participate in construction and development projects in the State because of their positive impact on the local economy, especially through attracting capital and transferring technology and knowledge in a way that enhances the efficiency of workers and raises the level of services provided, to provide the state’s growing electricity needs and improving the level of power generation in order to strengthen the existing grid and provide the basic infrastructure for the implementation of other State projects contained in its development plan and cover part of the future energy needs. Furthermore, to achieve competition in the electricity sectors and increase renewable energy capacity within the national energy mix.

## 3- Investment Period:
The Project Company (“Generator”) shall sign the Power Purchase Agreement (“PPA”) with MEWRE to export its production of electricity to the MEWRE grid for 30 years from the Project Commercial Operation Date (“PCOD”).

## 4- Contractual Framework:
The PPP agreements shall contain legal and commercial conditions governing the work of the Project, including the following terms and conditions:
- The development, financing, design, procurement, engineering, construction, testing, and commissioning of the plant and the 400 kV transmission substation for the export of electrical power.
- Ownership, operation, and maintenance of the plant by the Project Company (Generator).
- Terms that will regulate the sale and purchase of electricity between the Project Company (the Generator and the buyer and terms and conditions of the payment to the Project Company (Generator).
- Deductions and damages to the Project Company (Generator in case of breach of the terms and conditions of the PPA and any other damages.
- Conditions and procedures for the transfer of ownership of the project’s assets and personnel upon expiration of the contract period to the State, including requirements for the delivery of assets and the project to the State.

Other significant agreements will include but are not limited to (Letter Agreement, Step-in-rights Agreement, Land Lease Agreements for the use of the Project site and temporary areas and Shareholders’ Agreement for the establishment and management of the Project Company (Generator).

## 5- Submission of proposal:
Prior to receiving the Request for Proposals, a confidentiality agreement in the form specified by KAPP must be obtained, signed, and returned to KAPP by the Qualified Bidders.
The Qualified Bidders are invited to purchase the RFP package through a payment of 7,000 KWD (Seven Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) for Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects.
Payment can be made using any of the following options:
a. Online transfer via IBAN to KW07CBKU0000000000000012012039 (payment shall be net of charges and may take around 3 (three) Business Days for internal processing at KAPP); or
b. Submit a non-refundable certified cheque issued from a licensed bank operating in Kuwait, in favour of ‘Kuwait Authority for Partnership Projects’; or
c. Payment through KNET machine (Visa/Mastercard not accepted).

For option (b) and (c), payment shall be submitted to:

The documents shall be returned after being completed, with the required documents attached inside, along with a preliminary bid bond of not less than (2%) of the bid value in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee issued by one of the accredited banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, issued in the name of the bidder and for the benefit of the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>, and not subject to any restriction or condition. Bids not accompanied by this bond will not be considered, even if they conform to the specifications. The bond must be valid for the required bid validity period. The documents shall be submitted in an official envelope sealed with red wax, and the bids will be delivered to the (Tenders and Contracts Department) at the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>.
Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is (one o'clock in the afternoon) on (Thursday), 03/07/2025. Any bid submitted after this deadline will be rejected.

Any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency will not be considered.

- In accordance with the text of Article 48 of the Public Tenders Law No. 49 of 2016, which states:
> "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session in the presence of the bidders or their representatives."

- In the event of purchasing the documents and paying the prescribed fees, requests for a refund of the fees will not be accepted except in the case of the practice being canceled in accordance with the provisions of Article (55) of the Public Tenders Law.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the envelope opening session.
- Companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Section before the day scheduled for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1. A copy of the Civil ID.
2. A copy of the signature authorization specific to the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. In the event that someone other than the authorized signatory attends, a written letter from the person whose signature is authorized with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be brought, delegating whomever they see fit to attend the session.
- This announcement is an integral part of the practice documents.
- For more information, please visit our website at WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW

1- Tender documents can be obtained from the Procurement Department website (https://pur.ku.edu.kw)
2- The deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, 01/07/2025, at 12:00 PM. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session.
3- Instructions for Bidders:
- The bid must be submitted on optical discs (CDs) (3 copies), ensuring that all files have been copied correctly before placing the discs in the submission envelope. The copies must be identical, matching, protected, and non-modifiable, and each must contain all tender documents signed and stamped with the bidder's (company's) seal.
- Inquiries will be accepted for 10 days from the date of the announcement. No inquiries will be accepted after the specified deadline.
- The following hard copy documents must be submitted:
  - The original copy of the bid and undertaking form.
  - The initial bid bond (as per the tender announcement).
  - The purchase receipt from the website.
  - A copy of a valid and effective national labor percentage certificate.
  - A valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no holds on the bidder's file.
  - The envelope designated for the tender.
- The bid will be disqualified if any document mentioned in the instructions is not submitted.
1- Bids shall be placed in the designated box at the Procurement Department – in Sabah Al-Salem University City (Al-Shadadiya) <orig>مدينة صباح السالم الجامعية ( الشدادية )</orig> – University Administration Building – Sixth Floor – Supplier Affairs Section.
**Note:**
Tender documents may be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the university's Supplier Affairs Section and with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, during official working hours.

# Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>
## Announcement

The Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig> announces the submission by:

<table_caption>Details of Companies Involved in the Economic Concentration Request</table_caption>
<table>
| Company | Activity |
|:---|:---|
| ACWA Power Company <orig>شركة أكوا باور</orig> | Activity: Generation of electrical power, wholesale distribution and sale of electrical power, water desalination, repair and maintenance of power generation plants and transformers, and sale of desalinated water. |
| AZN Dutch Holdco No. 1 B.V. <orig>شركة إيه زد إن دتش هولدكو رقم 1. بي. في.</orig> | Activity: Holding company. |
| AZN Dutch Holdco No. 2 B.V. <orig>شركة إيه زد إن دتش هولدكو رقم 2. بي. في.</orig> | Activity: Holding company. |
| AZN O&M Company W.L.L. <orig>شركة إي زد أن أو اند أم ذ.م.م</orig> | Activity: Operation, supply, development, and maintenance of electrical power and desalinated drinking water. |
</table>

<image_caption>ACWA Power Logo</image_caption>
<image>
{
  "description": "The logo for ACWA Power, with the name in both English and Arabic.",
  "type": "logo",
  "data": "ACWA POWER, أكوا باور"
}
</image>

<image_caption>AZN O&M Company W.L.L. Logo</image_caption>
<image>
{
  "description": "The logo for AZN O&M Company W.L.L., with the name in both English and Arabic.",
  "type": "logo",
  "data": "AZN O&M COMPANY W.L.L, إي زد أن أو اند أم ذ.م.م"
}
</image>

of a request for approval to complete an economic concentration transaction

The acquisition by ACWA Power Company <orig>شركة أكوا باور</orig> of 100% of the shares of AZN Dutch Holdco No. 1 B.V. <orig>شركة إيه زد إن دتش هولدكو رقم 1. بي. في.</orig> and 50% of the shares of AZN O&M Company W.L.L. <orig>شركة إي زد أن أو اند أم ذ.م.م</orig>, owned by Kahrabel (S.P.C.) <orig>شركة كهربيل (م.م.ح)</orig>.

In accordance with Law No. (72) of 2020 regarding Competition Protection and Article (83) of its Executive Regulations issued by Resolution No. (14) of 2021 and its amendments, which stipulates that "Any interested party may submit a reasoned objection to the Agency regarding the economic concentration request within (15) fifteen days from the date of notification or publication..."

Accordingly, the Agency invites any interested party to submit its reasoned objection to this economic concentration within a period not exceeding fifteen days from the date of this announcement.

Objection details shall be submitted at the headquarters of the Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>, Al Hamra Tower, 14th floor, by filling out the form available on the website and paying the prescribed fee.

http://www.cpa.gov.kw
info@cpa.gov.kw
@cpakwt
@cpa_kw

1. The aforementioned fee must be paid only via "K-Net" at the Institution's treasury.
2. Bids shall be submitted to the main headquarters of the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> in Mirqab <orig>المرقاب</orig>, in the tender box located on the ground floor. The deadline for submitting bids is one o'clock in the afternoon.

To submit any reservations or inquiries regarding the aforementioned tender, please send them by email no later than Wednesday, 25/6/2025. Requests submitted after this date will not be considered:
Procurement@pifss.gov.kw

The following documents must be submitted when purchasing the tender documents:
1. An authorization letter from the company containing the name and Civil ID number of the person authorized to purchase the tender documents.
2. A copy of the Civil ID card of the person authorized to purchase the tender documents.

Additionally, copies of the following documents must be enclosed inside the bid envelope:
1. A recent copy of the company's license from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
2. A recent copy of the registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. A recent copy of the certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>.
4. A clearance certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there are no suspension codes on the tenderer's file with the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, addressed to the Institution and specific to the tender being offered.
5. A certificate of payment of contributions to the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الإجتماعية</orig>.
6. A copy of the registration form in the register of contractors, suppliers, and providers at the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الإجتماعية</orig>.

- The deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 10/7/2025, at exactly one o'clock in the afternoon, local time of the State of Kuwait (1:00 PM), noting that the bid must be submitted through the commercial e-platform mentioned above.
- The practitioner must submit the initial guarantee in favor of the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> in an envelope bearing the name and address of the practice and the closing date. It must be placed in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, at the main office building in Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>, no later than one o'clock in the afternoon (1:00 PM) on Thursday, 10/7/2025, with a copy of the initial guarantee attached to the bid.
- Note that this practice is general and divisible, with supply to be from the unified qualification list of the Central Qualification Committee <orig>لجنة التأهيل المركزية</orig>.
- A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid in a tender, with the exception of alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
- However, a person who has a share in separate companies, where each company is independent in its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative structure, may, upon classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.
- A bidder's bid that violates this article shall be considered null and void by rule of law, in accordance with Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders.
- Note: –
- All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the platform and the practice documents.
- The Internal Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء الداخلية</orig> would like to draw the attention of practitioners who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit these requests a maximum of (two weeks) before the closing date (for this practice). Such requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason after this deadline.
- To obtain a username and password to access the commercial e-platform, please call the telephone numbers 23887793/23887794
cwphlp@knpc.com.kw
- Explanatory instructions on how to submit a bid through the commercial e-platform are available on our website.

Secretary

## Announcement
Annual Plan for Supply, Contracting, and Service Contracts
Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that in accordance with Article No. (33) and Article No. (88) of the Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016 regarding the subject of the above announcement, the plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>. Therefore, all those interested in viewing them should visit the website continuously to get the latest updates by following the steps below:
1- The company's website WWW.KOCKW.COM
2- Click on E-business
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFPs) and Procurements (RFQs)
4- Click on Upcoming
